# CartFlow — System Summary (Architecture)

## 1) System Overview

CartFlow is a FastAPI application that:

- Embeds a storefront **widget** (JavaScript) for hesitation / exit-intent UX and **reason capture**.
- Receives **cart lifecycle events** (e.g. abandon, conversion) via **`POST /api/cart-event`** and schedules **delayed WhatsApp recovery** (Twilio path in `services/whatsapp_send.py`; Meta Cloud API path in `main.send_whatsapp_message` for interactive CTA messages used elsewhere).
- Persists **store settings**, **abandoned carts**, **recovery reasons**, and **recovery logs** in SQLAlchemy models (`models.py`), with optional schema patches via `schema_widget.py`.
- Serves **merchant dashboards** as Jinja2 HTML under `/dashboard/*`, loading/saving settings through **`GET`/`POST /api/recovery-settings`** and related APIs.
- **`GET /`** — public marketing landing (`templates/cartflow_landing.html`): Arabic RTL **product-story landing** — behavior + objection + recovery + explanation (hero flow, real dashboard screenshots for objection reasons / recovery templates / carts / widget / WhatsApp); no fake ROI; CTAs **`/signup`** and **`/login`**.

**Institutional memory (V1):** long-term architecture knowledge — ownership, decisions, failures, governance, dependencies — in **`docs/institutional_memory/`** (index: `README.md`). Audit baseline: Purchase Truth, Lifecycle Truth, Data Growth, Snapshot Governance **CLOSED**; Meta **PENDING**.

**Product Investigation Framework V1:** after Reality Validation Lab V1, significant weaknesses become permanent **Investigation Cases** (INV-*), not bugs — evidence, RCA, severity, owner, verification, closure criteria; **no symptom fixes** until Architectural review marks Ready for Fix. Registry: **`docs/investigations/`** (INV-001 Time Authority, INV-002 Merchant Identity, … INV-008 Visitor Truth). Wave 0 parents before children. **No Phase 4 / no implementation from this phase.**

**Lifecycle Exit Criteria Framework V1** (`LIFECYCLE_EXIT_CRITERIA_FRAMEWORK_V1.md`): permanent Exit Criteria for Constitution → … → Closure. Peer to Execution Governance. **Approved.**

**Merchant Trust Constitution V1** · **Identity Authority Architecture V1** · **INV-002 Execution Architecture** — **Approved.** **INV-002 DoR: READY FOR FIX.** **WP-1** foundation · **WP-2** Knowledge MQIC · **WP-3** Session & membership binding (`session_membership_v1`; Knowledge bind delegates); review `WP-03_REVIEW.md`. **`main.py` untouched. STOP — await Architecture approval before WP-4.**  

**Investigations / Phase Review:** INV-001 WP-1…WP-6 approved; INV-002 Root Cause Confirmed; Phase Review V1 decision **A — Continue INV-002** (governance only). Admin: `/admin/investigations`.

### 1.1 Commercial packaging (approved foundation — audit only, no billing)

| Package | Monthly (SAR) | Annual (SAR) | Target merchant |
|---------|---------------|--------------|-----------------|
| **Starter** | 99 | 990 | Entry — widget, reason capture, single-path WhatsApp recovery, dashboard, basic analytics, default templates |
| **Growth** (Most Popular) | 199 | 1,990 | Active stores — adds VIP detection/alerts, multi-message, per-reason templates/timing, advanced analytics, merchant controls |
| **Pro** | 399 | 3,990 | High maturity — advanced recovery/message logic, operational insights, early access, future intelligence modules |

**Pricing model:** feature-based; monthly + annual; **no message/recovery quotas** in marketing (internal fair usage may apply later). Pricing audit: **`docs/cartflow_packages_pricing_foundation_audit_v1.md`**.

**SaaS foundation Phase 1 (implemented — no payment processing):** canonical plans + entitlements (`services/cartflow_plans_v1.py`, `services/cartflow_entitlements_v1.py`); subscription state on **`MerchantUser`** (`current_plan`, `plan_status`, `plan_source`, `plan_started_at`, `plan_expires_at`); `GET /api/merchant/subscription` + read-only dashboard card; marketplace event vocabulary (`zid_plan_*`, `salla_plan_*` — architecture only). Enforcement via **`CARTFLOW_PLAN_ENTITLEMENTS_ENFORCE`** (default off). Audit: **`docs/cartflow_saas_foundation_phase1_marketplace_plan_system_audit_v1.md`**.

**SaaS foundation Phase 2 (pricing & subscription UI — visual only):** enhanced current-plan card on `#settings`; read-only plans comparison page `#plans` (Starter/Growth/Pro features + SAR pricing); `GET /api/merchant/plans-catalog`; `merchant_plans_ui.js`; topbar «الباقة» → `#plans`. No upgrade/billing/checkout. Visual proof: `scripts/_saas_plans_ui_out/`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_plans_ui_v1.py`.

**SaaS foundation Phase 3 (trial & admin subscription control):** Admin `/admin/subscriptions/control` — manual plan/trial assignment, audit log, merchant dashboard reflects Trial status; no billing. Doc: **`docs/cartflow_saas_foundation_phase3_trial_admin_subscription_control_audit_v1.md`**.

**SaaS foundation Phase 3.1 (automatic subscription dates):** `billing_interval` (`trial` / `monthly` / `annual` / `manual_custom`); admin preset actions auto-compute dates (14 / 30 / 365 days); custom dates only for `manual_custom`; enriched audit log; merchant dashboard shows interval + trial/plan expiry; marketplace date helper (`merchant_billing_interval_v1.py`). Doc: **`docs/cartflow_saas_foundation_phase3_1_automatic_subscription_dates_audit_v1.md`**.

**Marketplace Subscription Sync v1 (architecture audit only):** Six event types (`zid_plan_*`, `salla_plan_*` including `*_cancelled`); normalized adapter contract → `MerchantUser` field mapping; store linkage; idempotent receipts + audit log; admin fallback; failure taxonomy. No webhooks implemented. Doc: **`docs/cartflow_marketplace_subscription_sync_v1_audit.md`**.

**SaaS foundation Phase 4 (subscription experience):** Subscription Status Card V2 (plan/status/source badges, days remaining, health messages); current plan benefits + read-only upgrade discovery; admin list shows days remaining + health. No billing/checkout/enforcement. Doc: **`docs/cartflow_saas_foundation_phase4_subscription_experience_audit_v1.md`**.

### 1.2 Merchant value foundation (contract — docs only)

**Value Validation Foundation V1:** defines **why merchants pay CartFlow** and **how CartFlow proves value** — the bridge between engineering excellence (`docs/engineering_constitution_v1.md`) and commercial success (retention, expansion, pricing, trust). **Not** Merchant Intelligence or Knowledge Layer implementation. Six permanent **value domains** (Revenue Recovery, Customer Understanding, Product Understanding, Store Health, Operational Confidence, Decision Support); four **proof categories** (Recovery, Understanding, Decision, Operational); nine **evidence types** (Purchase/Lifecycle/Recovery/Provider/Behavior/Product Truth, Knowledge Layer, Integration/Read Model Truth); **Daily Brief** contract (3–5 insights, what/why/action); value measurement scorecard; commercial impact matrix; roadmap alignment from closed engineering (Purchase Truth → Recovery Proof, LT-C1 → Customer Understanding, Provider Reliability → Operational Confidence, Dashboard Read Model → Merchant Visibility, etc.); future domains listed (purpose only). Doc: **`docs/cartflow_value_validation_foundation_v1.md`**. Related audits: **`docs/cartflow_merchant_decision_summary_v1.md`** (current decision confidence **C−** baseline).

**Merchant Value Audit V1:** read-only audit of **current merchant-facing value** against the value validation contract — 16 merchant-visible capabilities inventoried; evidence classification (Confirmed/Partial/Future); 17 merchant questions mapped (1 answered, 12 partial, 4 not); proof maturity (Understanding strongest ~L1–2, Decision weakest ~L0–1); commercial readiness **Partially Ready** for pilot / **Not Ready** for ROI/self-serve; unique outcomes (reason-at-hesitation, LT-C1 decision frame, VIP merchant alert, honest attribution discipline); top gaps (attributed SAR, intervention actions, daily brief, delivery truth); overall **Level 1 Working**; recommends next foundation: **Proof of Value**. Doc: **`docs/merchant_value_audit_v1.md`**.

**Proof of Value Foundation V1:** ratified **commercial counterpart** to `engineering_constitution_v1.md` — defines what CartFlow **may claim**, how value is **measured**, and how value is **presented** (not implementation/UI/marketing). **§1 Proof Philosophy** (Truth Before Claims, Evidence Before Marketing, Proof Before Intelligence, Measured Before Estimated, Merchant Trust Before Growth). **§2 five proof domains** (Recovery, Understanding, Decision, Operational, Commercial) with required evidence. **§3 evidence hierarchy** Tier 0–4 (Purchase/Lifecycle/Provider/Recovery/Widget Truth → Behavior/Product/Integration/Read Model → KL → AI Explanation → Presentation); presentation and AI never create evidence. **§4 contracts PV-1…PV-18** (evidence-backed claims, attribution, delivery≠sent, confidence, unknown stays unknown, tier alignment, daily brief, eligible actions). **§5 merchant proof surfaces** (carts, home, daily brief, timeline, monthly, setup, reports, mobile — purpose only). **§6 value metrics** (Recovered Revenue, Recovery Rate, Known Reasons, Decision/Operational Confidence, etc.) with merchant-visible today column. **§7 confidence model** (Confirmed/High/Medium/Low/Unknown). **§8 commercial integrity** (forbidden claims CI-1…CI-10; tier matrix). **§9–§10** roadmap + evolution/amendment. Baseline: Merchant Value Audit **Level 1 Working**. Doc: **`docs/proof_of_value_foundation_v1.md`**.

**Proof of Value Governance V1:** authoritative **governed domain contract** — converts foundation PV-* into enforceable governance (peer to Provider Reliability Governance, Dashboard Read Model Governance). **§1 principles PG-1…PG-10** (Truth Before Claims, Evidence Before Confidence, Proof Before Presentation, Commercial Integrity Before Growth, Unknown Remains Unknown, Governance Before Surfacing). **§2 proof ownership** — truth / presentation / governance owner per domain (Recovery, Understanding, Decision, Operational, Commercial) mapped to existing modules. **§3 proof lifecycle** Truth→Evidence→Proof→Merchant Surface→Commercial Value with stage write rules. **§4 governance contracts PV-1…PV-18** — each with owner, verification method, merchant impact, risk P0–P3; audit traceability + open compliance baseline. **§5 merchant trust rules** (confidence, uncertainty, attribution, delivery, recommendations, unknown). **§6 commercial integrity** CI-1…CI-10 + pilot whitelist + release gate. **§7 measurement** — proof coverage, confidence quality, metric registry governance, domain maturity L0–L6, phased P0–P3 compliance targets. **§8 evolution** — new domains/contracts without weakening principles. Domain enters **Level 2 Governed** on adoption; merchant value remains **Level 1 Working** until implementation. Doc: **`docs/proof_of_value_governance_v1.md`**.

**Proof Surface Implementation V1 (Value Delivery Era — presentation only):** `services/merchant_proof_surface_v1.py` + cart row attach in `main.py` + dashboard/KL render. Read-only composition of existing Purchase/Lifecycle/Recovery/Provider Truth into `merchant_proof_surface_v1` on normal-carts rows (recovery steps: scheduled → message accepted → provider delivered [Unknown unless WhatsAppDeliveryTruth] → purchased → stopped; confidence weakest-link; `proof_source=recovery_key`). `#carts` row detail renders proof inside collapsed **MXP-5** timeline (`merchantProofSurfaceTimelineHtml` in `merchant_dashboard_lazy.js`). KL cards show per-card **الثقة · المصدر** via claim-level `evidence_id` (Claim-Level Evidence Ownership V1). Snapshot slim allowlist extended. **No** truth/recovery/scheduler/provider/snapshot/read-model logic changes. PV-11/CI-3 compliant. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_proof_surface_v1.py`. Doc: **`docs/proof_surface_implementation_v1.md`**.

**Merchant Evidence Registry Foundation V1:** `services/merchant_evidence_registry_v1.py` — permanent governed registry of stable `evidence_id` → merchant Arabic labels with `evidence_origin` (`store` = merchant-operational facts, `platform` = CartFlow-composed intelligence). **Claim-Level Evidence Ownership V1:** `services/merchant_claim_evidence_v1.py` — each KL insight owns its own `evidence_id` (no section-level proof); maps `insight_key` → registry; API enriches per card. **Registry Normalization V1:** one `evidence_id` = one origin + one merchant meaning (`customer_response` split → `hesitation_reason` / `customer_reply`). Proof Surface + KL consume normalized registry. JS reads claim/registry payload only. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_evidence_registry_v1.py`, `tests/test_merchant_claim_evidence_v1.py`. Docs: **`docs/merchant_evidence_registry_foundation_v1.md`**, **`docs/claim_level_evidence_ownership_v1.md`**, **`docs/merchant_evidence_registry_normalization_v1.md`**.

**Merchant Decision Foundation V1:** `docs/merchant_decision_foundation_v1.md` — permanent decision architecture for Merchant Value (foundation only — no implementation, scoring, AI, UI, or Daily Brief code). Defines Truth→Evidence→Proof→**Decision**→Merchant Action→Business Outcome chain; permanent separation of **observation / decision / recommendation / action**; decision classes (Observation → Needs Attention → Suggested Action → Critical Action); mandatory decision contract (Decision ID, type, evidence, confidence, action, business goal, owner, verification); merchant attention model + silence rules; commercial alignment (recover revenue, reduce hesitation, improve conversion, reduce workload, increase confidence, improve operations). Future Daily Brief, Decision Engine, notifications, and recommendations **must implement** this foundation. Subordinate cart design: **`docs/merchant_decision_layer_v1.md`**. Aligns with Proof of Value PV-4/17/18 and PG-2/3/5.

**Merchant Decision Governance V1:** `docs/merchant_decision_governance_v1.md` — authoritative **governed decision contract** (peer to Proof of Value Governance) — owns **Decision stage only** in the pipeline. **DG-1…DG-10** principles (Decision Before Presentation, Proof Before Decision, Unknown Never Produces Action, Merchant Attention Is Protected, etc.); decision ownership (eligibility, confidence, priority, expiration, suppression, lifecycle); governed class matrix + attention budgets; testable **MD-1…MD-12** contracts; commercial goal enum; integration with Evidence Registry, Proof Surface, PoV Governance without duplication. Future Daily Brief, Decision Engine, notifications, AI summaries **must implement** this governance. **No** implementation, ranking, UI, or AI. Maturity target: Decision domain **L2 Governed** when Decision Engine ships.

**Merchant Decision Implementation V1:** `services/merchant_decision_layer_v1.py` + `services/merchant_decision_registry_v1.py` — governed decision **execution engine** (Proof → Decisions). Cart rows: `attach_merchant_decisions_v1` after proof surface (`main.py`); KL: `enrich_knowledge_report_merchant_decisions_v1` on `/api/knowledge/report`. Output `merchant_decisions_v1` with full contract (class, evidence_ids, proof_sources, confidence, commercial_goal, merchant_action, priority, expiration, suppression, lifecycle, explanation). V1-A `merchant_decision_key` unchanged. Governance-only priority; suppression (silent, already_addressed, merged, …). Observability: `get_merchant_decision_observability_v1()`. Snapshot allowlist includes `merchant_decisions_v1`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_decision_execution_v1.py`. Doc: **`docs/merchant_decision_implementation_v1.md`**. Consumed by Daily Brief V1.

**Merchant Daily Brief Foundation V1:** `docs/merchant_daily_brief_foundation_v1.md` — permanent Daily Brief architecture (foundation only — no implementation, UI, ranking, notifications, or AI). **First governed consumer of Merchant Decisions** — consumes `merchant_decisions_v1` **published** decisions only; never Truth/Evidence/Proof directly; never mints decisions. Answers: what happened / why it matters / what to do. Attention budget **3–5 items** (PV-18); silence acceptable. Principles DBP-1…DBP-11; brief item = projection of decision contract. Aligns with Decision Foundation/Governance + PV-18. **Not implemented.**

**Merchant Daily Brief Implementation V1:** `services/merchant_daily_brief_v1.py` + `routes/daily_brief.py` + `static/merchant_daily_brief.js` — first governed **consumer** of `merchant_decisions_v1`. `GET /api/dashboard/daily-brief` aggregates published decisions from cart rows + KL bundles; selects ≤5 by priority; projects what/why/action + confidence + evidence. Home `#ma-daily-brief-root` on overview. **UX Redesign V1:** briefing layout (greeting → hero → queue). **IA Redesign V1:** action-first hero; class as metadata; summary bootstrap (`merchant_daily_brief_v1` on `/api/dashboard/summary`); desktop grid queue. **Composer V2:** `services/merchant_daily_brief_composer_v2.py` — deterministic topic aggregation with **Aggregation Governance AG-1…AG-10** (achievements first, attention topics max 5; traceable `source_decision_ids`; no decision/truth changes). Doc: **`docs/merchant_daily_brief_composer_v2.md`**. Docs: **`docs/merchant_daily_brief_ux_redesign_v1.md`**, **`docs/merchant_daily_brief_ia_redesign_v1.md`**. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_daily_brief_v1.py`, `tests/test_merchant_daily_brief_composer_v2.py`. Does **not** mint decisions or read Truth directly.

**Merchant Explanation Unification V1:** `services/merchant_explanation_v1.py` — unified merchant explanation layer for all cart lifecycle states (presentation only — no Truth/Decision changes). Single `merchant_explanation_v1` bundle per cart row: sanitized Arabic copy, `diagnostic_internal` admin-only, Knowledge Routing prep metadata (`explanation_id`, `knowledge_event_type`, `eligible_surfaces`, `action_required`, `attention_level`). Cart detail JS reads explanation only; proof surface steps removed from merchant block. Wired in `main.py` after proof attach. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_explanation_v1.py`. Doc: **`docs/merchant_explanation_unification_v1.md`**. Upstream input to future Knowledge Routing.

**Knowledge Routing Foundation V1:** `docs/knowledge_routing_foundation_v1.md` — permanent routing architecture between Merchant Explanation / Decision and Surface Composition (foundation only — no implementation, UI, or surface changes). Knowledge Routing owns **Eligibility · Prioritization · Lifetime · Surface Visibility**. Defines platform-owned knowledge vs surface consumption; knowledge item + routed knowledge item contract (including `routing_priority`); surface vocabulary (10 surfaces); surface eligibility matrix; **Knowledge Prioritization Governance KP-1…KP-10** (platform-owned attention order; surfaces truncate budgets but never re-rank; deterministic, no AI); merchant vs admin visibility; notification/aggregation/narrative eligibility; principles **KR-1…KR-12**. Worked examples: return-without-purchase, repeated shipping hesitation, purchase confirmed. Future surfaces must consume pre-prioritized routed knowledge — not independently select or reorder display content.

**Knowledge Routing Readiness Review V1:** `docs/knowledge_routing_readiness_review_v1.md` — pre-implementation architectural validation (docs only). Inventories knowledge sources (Truth / Explanation / Decision / Presentation); audits surface ownership (Cart Detail, Daily Brief, Home, KL, Monthly, Notifications); assesses Explanation + Decision + Composer V2 readiness; maps contract gaps; lists 11 active surface-selection violations; migration plan Phase 0–3; risks. **Verdict: C — architecture gaps remain** (Composer V2 + KL JS own interim routing-like logic; decision routing metadata missing). Phase 0 doc closures required before Implementation V1; first consumer target = Daily Brief via Composer migration.

**Knowledge Production Standardization V1:** `docs/knowledge_production_standardization_v1.md` — ratified Phase 0 standard closing Readiness Review Verdict C (docs only — no routing engine, UI, or behavior changes). Defines governed **Knowledge Producers** (Explanation, Decision, Proof, KL; excludes JS/templates/widgets/Composer); **Knowledge Publisher Contract** (18 required fields); deterministic **`knowledge_id`** convention (`expl:…`, `dec:…`, `kl:…`); producer readiness matrix; **surface selection freeze** (no new `if purchase/return/hesitation` in surfaces); metadata gap closure per producer; migration sequence Steps 1–7 before/during Routing V1; governance **KPUB-1…KPUB-10**. Routing Implementation V1 must not begin until producer metadata is implemented per §6.

**Knowledge Producer Metadata Implementation V1:** `services/knowledge_producer_metadata_v1.py` — producer-side publisher contract (metadata only — no routing, no UI/behavior changes). Shared deterministic `knowledge_id` + `traceability`; enriches **`merchant_explanation_v1`**, each **`merchant_decisions_v1`** decision, and KL **`insights[]`** via `/api/knowledge/report`. Fields: `knowledge_version`, `knowledge_id`, `knowledge_type`, `source_domain`, evidence/proof/decision/explanation links, confidence, visibility, surfaces, attention, aggregation, narrative, expiration, traceability. Tests: `tests/test_knowledge_producer_metadata_v1.py`. Doc: **`docs/knowledge_producer_metadata_implementation_v1.md`**.

**Knowledge Routing Implementation V1:** `services/knowledge_routing_v1.py` — first platform-owned routing layer (domain-neutral; metadata-only). Consumes standardized producer items; assigns **`routing_priority`**; aggregates by producer **`aggregation_key`**; outputs routed knowledge items with full traceability. **Phase 1 consumer:** `merchant_daily_brief_composer_v2.py` — projection-only (routing owns select/rank/filter/aggregate; Composer projects headlines from `knowledge_payload`). Wired in `build_merchant_daily_brief_api_payload()`. Brief payload includes `knowledge_routing_v1` observability. **No** Truth/Decision/Explanation/UI changes. Tests: `tests/test_knowledge_routing_v1.py`, `tests/test_merchant_daily_brief_composer_v2.py`. Doc: **`docs/knowledge_routing_implementation_v1.md`**. Future phases: KL, Home, Cart Detail, Notifications, Monthly Summary.

**Merchant Knowledge Infrastructure Closure Review V1:** `docs/merchant_knowledge_infrastructure_closure_review_v1.md` — **finalized** architectural certification closing the Merchant Knowledge Infrastructure era (review only). Certifies integrated pipeline Truth → Evidence → Proof → Decision → Explanation → Producer → Routing → Projection → Surface. Includes **Merchant Knowledge Infrastructure Declaration** and **Permanent Architectural Rule** (no second knowledge pipeline; parallel ownership prohibited). **Verdict B** — infrastructure architecturally complete; remaining work is consumer migration (KL JS, Cart Detail, Merchant Home) — not infrastructure gaps. Daily Brief certified first full routing consumer. Future features extend governed infrastructure as consumers only.

**Permanent Architectural Rule (Merchant Knowledge):** No future feature may introduce a second merchant knowledge pipeline. Every new capability must integrate into the existing Merchant Knowledge Infrastructure. Parallel knowledge ownership is permanently prohibited. Ratified in **`docs/merchant_knowledge_infrastructure_closure_review_v1.md`**.

**Merchant Experience Foundation V1:** `docs/merchant_experience_foundation_v1.md` — **opens Era 2** (Merchant Experience) after Merchant Knowledge Infrastructure closure (Era 1). Merchant Experience = governed presentation of platform knowledge — not a collection of screens; experience expresses infrastructure, never replaces it. **Mission:** reduce merchant thinking; answer what happened / what to do / did CartFlow handle this before the merchant asks. **Principles ME-1…ME-8** (consume not recreate; reduce thinking not reading; protect attention; CartFlow acts first; reflect architecture; calm before information; achievements before problems; no KPI walls). **Merchant day model** (morning open → achievements → today's actions → leave → notifications → weekly → monthly). **Ten surfaces** defined (Home, Daily Brief, Weekly Brief, Monthly Summary, Notifications, KL, Cart Detail, Mobile, Executive, AI) — each with why/when/experience/knowledge consumed/must-never-own. **Merchant Experience Pyramid** (Trust → Awareness → Attention → Decision → Improvement). **Architectural rules** extend Permanent Architectural Rule — experience consumes, never owns Truth/Evidence/Proof/Decision/Explanation/Routing/Production. **Merchant Experience Era Declaration** at document end. **Not implemented** — foundation only; no UI, routing migration, AI, or cadence builds.

**Merchant Experience Migration Program V1:** `docs/merchant_experience_migration_program_v1.md` — **first operational program of Era 2** (migration only — not feature sprint). Mission: one platform intelligence across all surfaces; every surface **Infrastructure Consumer, never Infrastructure Owner**. **Phases:** 0 Daily Brief (certified reference) → **Phase 1 Knowledge Layer** ✅ → **Phase 2 Cart Detail** ✅ → **Phase 3 Merchant Home** ✅ (`docs/merchant_home_experience_v1.md`). MEM-1…MEM-6; per-surface certification checklist. **Program complete** — all three migration phases certified. Weekly/Monthly/Notifications/Executive/AI unblocked for Era 2 expansion. **Certification: PASS** (Phases 1–3).

**Merchant Home Experience V1 (Graduation Sprint — Phase 3 complete):** `docs/merchant_home_experience_v1.md`. `services/merchant_home_composition_v1.py` composes five-section operating center from Daily Brief achievements/attention + Home-routed KL understanding + nav metadata; `merchant_home_experience.js` presentation-only; `#ma-home-experience-root` replaces dashboard widgets on overview; KPIs on `#page-home-month` only. **`route_merchant_home_knowledge_v1()`** for store understanding slice. **M1 Activation V1:** `services/merchant_home_experience_activation_v1.py` — transport-independent summary contract (`finalize_dashboard_summary_payload` on live + snapshot); read-time compose for pre-M1 snapshots; auto snapshot upgrade; `_merchant_home_transport` ops diagnostics. Doc: **`docs/merchant_home_experience_m1_activation_v1.md`**. **No** Truth/Decision/Explanation/routing algorithm changes. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_home_experience_v1.py`, `tests/test_merchant_home_experience_activation_v1.py`.

**Knowledge Layer Migration V1 (Sprint 1 — Phase 1 complete):** `docs/knowledge_layer_migration_v1.md`. Retired JS `INSIGHT_PRIORITY`, `pickTopInsights`, OIA builders; routing owns select/rank/aggregate; `knowledge_layer_projection_v1` owns OIA projection; `merchant_knowledge_layer.js` presentation-only. API `/api/knowledge/report` adds `knowledge_routing_v1` + `knowledge_layer_projection_v1`. Second certified routing consumer after Daily Brief. **No** Truth/Decision/Explanation/routing algorithm changes.

**Cart Detail Migration V1 (Sprint 2 — Phase 2 complete):** `docs/cart_detail_migration_v1.md`. Retired JS `merchantDecisionExecutable`, `MERCHANT_DECISION_LABEL_AR`, local decision allowlist; routing owns cart-scoped feed; `cart_detail_projection_v1` owns explanation/action/lifecycle display blocks; `merchant_dashboard_lazy.js` presentation-only. Normal-carts rows add `cart_detail_projection_v1` via `attach_cart_detail_projection_v1` in `main.py`. Third certified routing consumer after Daily Brief and Knowledge Layer. **No** Truth/Decision/Explanation/routing algorithm changes. Tests: `tests/test_cart_detail_migration_v1.py`.

**Merchant Experience Review Board V1 (first executive product review — docs only):** `docs/merchant_experience_review_board_v1.md`. Post-migration merchant-facing product review (not engineering/architecture). **Overall B−** — Home morning story strong (achievements → attention → understanding); activated merchants can answer daily questions; setup fragmentation, Carts cognitive cliff, absent commercial proof on Home, and no away-mode notifications prevent full «platform works while I'm away» mission. Scores: Experience B, Clarity B−, Trust B−, Commercial Value C+, Simplicity B−, Daily Workflow B. Baseline for future experience-first decisions.

**Merchant Experience Cohesion Program V1 (first product-quality program — docs only):** `docs/merchant_experience_cohesion_program_v1.md`. After Migration unified **ownership**, Cohesion unifies **feeling** — one continuous merchant conversation (MEC-1…MEC-7). **Whisper Principle:** Home whispers; every surface must whisper; Carts list = Priority 1 cohesion fail. Program phases 0–6: Carts whisper → Setup one-chapter → Cart Detail/KL visual family → WhatsApp companion → Completed/wins separation → future Weekly/Notifications gate. Not architecture/features/routing/implementation.

**Merchant Experience Design Language V1 (permanent visual philosophy — docs only):** `docs/merchant_experience_design_language_v1.md`. Visual equivalent of Knowledge Routing Foundation — MDL-1…MDL-8; five-level hierarchy; five-second reading contract; Whisper Principle as whitespace/typography/color behavior; card philosophy; progressive disclosure; cognitive budget. Product Excellence implements this language; no per-screen local visual invention. Not Figma/CSS/component library.

**Merchant Experience Patterns V1 (permanent implementation patterns — docs only):** `docs/merchant_experience_patterns_v1.md`. Execution bridge Design Language → screen redesign — MXP-1…MXP-10 (Achievement, Attention, Waiting, Recovery Story, Timeline, Insight, Empty Knowledge, Empty Store, Suggested Action, Quick Navigation); composition rules; pattern certification per surface. Not UI/CSS/components/Figma.

**Merchant Experience Era Milestone M1 (closed — official baseline):** `docs/merchant_experience_era_milestone_m1.md`. Closes Merchant Experience Era foundation + migration. **Certified routing consumers:** Daily Brief, Knowledge Layer, Cart Detail, Merchant Home. Review Board B− + Cohesion Program established. **Transition:** platform construction → **Product Excellence** era. Commit: `feat: complete Merchant Experience Era milestone M1`.

**Merchant Intelligence Service V1 (constitutional intelligence layer — implemented):** `services/merchant_intelligence_v1.py` — single platform authority transforming Truth + Knowledge into Merchant Intelligence. Consumes published decisions, lifecycle/bucket truth, proof, explanation, VIP/phone signals. Produces four output families: **Intelligence Groups** (11 operational + pattern groups), **Recommendations** (derived from decision class + merchant-needed intervention projection), **Merchant Memory** (temporal comparison beats), **Merchant Priorities** (ordered attention bands). Per-cart attach: `attach_merchant_intelligence_v1` → `merchant_intelligence_v1` + `intelligence_group_key` on normal-carts rows (`main.py` after cart detail projection). Store attach: `attach_store_merchant_intelligence_v1` → `merchant_intelligence_store_v1` on `/api/dashboard/normal-carts`. **No UI/HTML/CSS/page knowledge.** Observability: `get_merchant_intelligence_observability_v1()`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_intelligence_v1.py` (18 pass). Doc: **`docs/merchant_intelligence_service_v1.md`**. Authority foundation: **`docs/merchant_intelligence_authority_foundation_v1.md`**. Surfaces consume read-only — Home/Carts/Brief/Notifications must not derive intelligence locally.

**Merchant Intelligence Consumption V1 — Carts Workspace (implemented):** First merchant-visible MI consumer. `static/merchant_intelligence_carts_v1.js` + `renderMiCartsV1Workspace()` in `merchant_dashboard_lazy.js`. Carts page prefers **`merchant_value_stories_v1`** (Merchant Value Composition Layer) over raw MI group text; groups remain internal. **UX V1:** stable expand, Arabic token mapping, four-question decision cards. **Transport:** `ensure_normal_carts_merchant_intelligence_store_v1()` + `ensure_normal_carts_merchant_value_stories_v1()` on read/write/live paths. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_intelligence_consumption_carts_v1.py`, `tests/test_merchant_intelligence_carts_ux_v1.py`, `tests/test_merchant_intelligence_snapshot_transport_v1.py`, `tests/test_merchant_value_composition_v1.py`. Docs: **`docs/merchant_intelligence_consumption_carts_v1.md`**, **`docs/merchant_value_composition_layer_v1.md`**. Wording authority: **`docs/cartflow_merchant_language_system_v1.md`**.

**Product Design System V1 (Product Design Constitution — docs only):** `docs/cartflow_product_design_system_v1.md` (**PDS-1.1**). Permanent visual law for how merchant value is communicated — principles for typography, currency/numbers, card/story hierarchy, buttons, whitespace, color, icons, layout, interaction, readability, accessibility. **Constitution governs consistency; Design Certification governs replaceable implementation** (typeface, palette, icons, tokens). PDS-11: no vendor-specific hard-coding. Complements Merchant Experience Design Language V1 (philosophy). Sits above implementation; no CSS/HTML/JS. Incorporates 2026-07-07 product review inputs (rejected «اكتملت مشتريات», default `449 ر.س` representation, story-title dominance, button subordination). §1.2 updated.

**Visual Identity Unification V1 (merchant presentation — implemented):** `static/merchant_visual_identity_v1.css` on PDS compliance stack. One product feel: certified Arial typography token (`--cfvi-font-certified`), unified card family, premium hero language (`ma-vi-hero`), semantic palette, hero-grade app bar + sidebar chrome, spacing rhythm, CTA hierarchy, motion. Hardening pass: WhatsApp/Plans/Settings cards unified; no dashed legacy cards; Plans teal accent; typography token enforcement. `syncVisualHero()` + updated `PAGE_PURPOSE` in `merchant_app.js`. Review: `scripts/_visual_identity_v1_prod_gate.py`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_visual_identity_v1.py`. PO approval required before closure.

**Typography Lock V1 (merchant presentation — implemented):** `static/merchant_typography_certification_v1.css` — final typography certification layer on VI stack. Single Arial typeface; 14 certified role tokens (`--cftyp-*`); universal lock overrides legacy `merchant_app.css` / PE v2 drift; hero subtitles unified; buttons/badges/sidebar/table/numeric/currency scales frozen. Removed Google Fonts IBM Plex from dashboard shell; inline font declarations cleaned from template + lazy JS. Report: `docs/cartflow_typography_certification_v1_report.md`. Review: `scripts/_typography_certification_v1_review.py`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_typography_certification_v1.py`. PO approval required before closure.

**PDS Final Closure V1 (merchant presentation — implemented):** Final Product Design System layer — `merchant_shell_identity_v1.css`, `merchant_card_system_v1.css`, `merchant_icon_language_v1.css`, `merchant_spacing_certification_v1.css` on typography stack. One shell, one card family (Carts reference), one icon language, one spacing rhythm. Body class `cf-pds-closure`. Review: `scripts/_visual_identity_final_review.py`. Tests: `tests/test_visual_identity_final_closure_v1.py`. Closes PDS V1; future work → Merchant Product Language only. PO approval required.

**Merchant Product Language V1 (Carts consumes MIL — presentation only):** `services/merchant_product_language_v1.py` + `merchant_product_language_templates.py` + `static/merchant_insight_layer_v1.js` + `static/merchant_product_language_v1.js`. MPL formats Merchant Insight output (`render_product_language_from_insight_v1`) — meaning owned by MIL; display order Insight → Reason → Action → Evidence. **Carts wired:** evidence → `compose_page_insight_v1` → MPL render above MI story cards. Legacy `compose_page_narrative_v1` for non-migrated pages only. Doc: **`docs/merchant_product_language_v1.md`**. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_product_language_v1.py`, `tests/test_merchant_product_language_carts_consumption_v1.py`.

**Merchant Insight Layer V1 (foundation — meaning before evidence):** `services/merchant_insight_layer_v1.py` + `merchant_insight_layer_templates.py` + `static/merchant_insight_layer_v1.js`. Governed composition layer; answers «What does this mean?» before evidence. Pipeline: **Insight → Reason → CartFlow Action → evidence_summary**. Carts + Home composers (Python); Carts client mirror. Certification: `validate_page_insight_v1()`. Doc: **`docs/merchant_insight_layer_v1.md`**. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_insight_layer_v1.py`.

**Lifecycle Governance Engine (LGE) V1 (interactive UI runtime — docs only):** Permanent browser-runtime governance architecture separating **policy from execution** for every interactive dashboard component. Stack: **Request → Lifecycle Registry → Lifecycle Governor → Lifecycle Controller → DOM Adapter → Browser**. Principles: One Lifecycle · One Governor · One Controller; policy never executes; controller never decides; DOM never owns state; browser is never authority; only Governor approves transitions. Formal state machine: CREATED → VISIBLE → EXPANDING → EXPANDED → UPDATING → COLLAPSING → VISIBLE → DESTROYED; lock system; governance events; violation taxonomy; phased migration (Phase 0 architecture → Phase 1 Story Cards → Timeline → Conversation Panel → Knowledge Cards → Widget → Dashboard components). **Story Cards are first consumer, not scope.** **No implementation, no code migration, no product changes.** Docs: **`docs/lifecycle_governance_engine_v1.md`**, **`docs/runtime_governance_rules_v1.md`**, **`docs/runtime_lifecycle_certification_v1.md`**. Current Story Cards baseline: **L0 Un governed** (distributed ownership in `merchant_intelligence_carts_v1.js` / `merchant_dashboard_lazy.js`).

**Responsive Layout Certification V1 (merchant presentation — implemented):** `static/merchant_responsive_layout_v1.css` — desktop layout families on `data-ma-page`: Family A medium width (Home, Store Setup, Monthly Summary); Family B full workspace (Carts, Messages, Activity/followup, Reasons); Family C comfort reading (WhatsApp, Widget, Plans, Settings). Identity/typography/spacing/hero unchanged; content container width only. Desktop `@media (min-width: 1024px)` only. Tests: `tests/test_responsive_layout_certification_v1.py`.

**Desktop Workspace Expansion Fix V1 (merchant presentation — implemented):** `static/merchant_workspace_expansion_v1.css` — fixes desktop white-space beside sidebar: removes duplicate sidebar reservation on `.ma-dashboard-frame` (shell `margin-right` + frame `right` double offset); expands data-page workspace shells (PE v2 `--v2-max-wide`, legacy `--ma-content-max` caps). Home Family A + Settings Family C unchanged. Desktop `@media (min-width: 1024px)` only. Review: `scripts/_workspace_expansion_visual_review_v1.py`. Tests: `tests/test_workspace_expansion_v1.py`.

**Currency Rendering Certification V2 (merchant presentation — implemented):** Single certified prefix format **`SR 449`** via `formatMerchantSar` / `formatMerchantSarHtml` (`merchant_pds_format_v1.js` + `services/merchant_pds_format_v1.py` Jinja filter). Atomic non-wrapping LTR currency atoms (`merchant_currency_certification_v1.css`). All manual `ر.س` / suffix / split-letter paths removed from merchant dashboard compact UI. Tests: `tests/test_currency_certification_v1.py`. Review: `scripts/_currency_sr_v2_visual_review_v1.py`.

## 2) Frontend Layer

### 2.1 Widget Layer (VERY IMPORTANT)

| Asset | Role |
|--------|------|
| `static/widget_loader.js` | Parses **`cartflowEarlyCartClickBootstrap`** at DCL (or immediately if document already interactive) — minimal capture-phase add-to-cart listener queues clicks before V2 loads; replayed by `zidCartEventSource` after bridge init. After **`window.load`**: schedules **`cartflow_return_tracker.js`**, then loads the widget. **Default storefront path:** layered **`cartflow_widget_runtime/cartflow_widget_loader.js`** (serial module chain) whenever **`window.__CARTFLOW_ALLOW_LEGACY_WIDGET !== true`** *or* **`window.CARTFLOW_WIDGET_RUNTIME_V2 === true`** (**`loadLayeredV2 = runtimeV2Explicit \|\| !legacyExplicit`** in shim). **Legacy `cartflow_widget.js`** loads **only** when **`__CARTFLOW_ALLOW_LEGACY_WIDGET === true`** **and** **`CARTFLOW_WIDGET_RUNTIME_V2` is not** `true` (rollback / QA — console **`[CF LEGACY WIDGET LOAD ALLOWED]`** vs **`[CF LEGACY WIDGET LOAD BLOCKED]`**). **`/demo/store*`** sets **`CARTFLOW_WIDGET_RUNTIME_V2 = true`** in the shim (**`cartflowIsDemoStorePrimaryV2Path()`**); **`templates/demo_store.html`** also sets **`CARTFLOW_WIDGET_RUNTIME_V2`** before the shim. Merchant dashboard embed (**`general_settings.html`**) references **`widget_loader.js` only** → **production default is V2**, not legacy. Skips tracker/widget bootstrap when session marked converted via `sessionStorage` / `cartflowIsSessionConverted`. Duplicate script detection skips re-injecting if runtime or legacy URL already present. |
| `static/cartflow_widget_runtime/*.js` | **Layered V2** storefront widget (config → API → state → triggers → **storefront cart bridge** → cart sources → cart event bridge → phone → shell → UI → flows → legacy_bridge). Starts via **`Flows.start()`** after bootstrap. Does **not** append **`cartflow_widget.js`** at runtime; VIP mirrors use **`mirrorCartTotals()`** in **`cartflow_widget_flows.js`** only. |
| `static/cartflow_widget.js` | **Legacy monolith** (`B`): **not** the default shim branch — loads only with **explicit** **`window.__CARTFLOW_ALLOW_LEGACY_WIDGET === true`** while **`CARTFLOW_WIDGET_RUNTIME_V2` is not** `true`, or via **`GET /dev/widget-test*`** (**`main._DEV_LEGACY_WIDGET_HARNESS_HTML`**, **`ENV=development`** only — **not** in **`_DEV_ROUTES_ALLOWED_WHEN_NOT_DEVELOPMENT`**). Retained for **rollback**, **dev harness**, and **static/operational test reads** (`tests/**` grep static file). **`/demo/store*`** does **not** load this asset in the happy path. |
| `static/cartflow_return_tracker.js` | Loaded by **`widget_loader.js`** (return-to-site / behavioral handoff signalling). |
| `static/cart_abandon_tracking.js` | Included from dashboard templates (`partials/cart_abandon_tracking.html`) for analytics-style tracking where wired. |

**Primary backend calls from storefront widgets:**

- **V2 (`cartflow_widget_fetch.js`, namespace `Api`):** `POST /api/cartflow/reason`, `GET /api/cartflow/ready`, `GET /api/cartflow/public-config` (`routes/cartflow.py`).
- **Legacy (`cartflow_widget.js`):** `POST /api/cart-recovery/reason` — persist widget **Layer D** (`routes/cart_recovery_reason.py`); `POST /api/cartflow/reason` alternate path (`routes/cartflow.py`).
- Shared / either surface as wired: `GET /api/recovery/primary-reason` — `main.py`; `POST /api/cartflow/generate-whatsapp-message` — mock WhatsApp preview (no DB write in that handler).

**Cart abandon signal to backend:** the storefront integration is expected to call **`POST /api/cart-event`** with `event: cart_abandoned` (handled in `main.handle_cart_abandoned` → recovery dispatch). The widget focuses on reasons and UX; the actual **abandon event** is typically from page / platform integration.

### 2.1.1 Widget architecture — operational posture (audit 2026-05)

| Topic | Assessment |
|--------|------------|
| **Default production behavior** | **Layered V2** via **`widget_loader.js`** without any global legacy opt-in (evidence: **`templates/general_settings.html`** embed = `widget_loader.js` only; shim **`loadLayeredV2`** true when **`__CARTFLOW_ALLOW_LEGACY_WIDGET` is not** set). |
| **Demo / primary V2 enforcement** | **`demo_store.html`** sets **`CARTFLOW_WIDGET_RUNTIME_V2`** + **`CARTFLOW_RUNTIME_VERSION`** before shim; shim **also** forces V2 on **`^/demo/store(/|$)`**. Baseline tests: **`tests/test_v2_widget_baseline_lock.py`**, **`tests/test_demo_behavioral_navigation.py`**. |
| **`cartflow_widget_runtime` load model** | **`cartflow_widget_loader.js`** loads modules **sequentially** (`async: false` tags, ordered **config → api → state → arbitration → theme → triggers → storefront cart bridge (contract/adapters/core) → cart_sources → cart_event_bridge → phone → shell → ui → flows → legacy_bridge**), then **`__cartflowV2Bootstrap` / `Flows.start()`**. **`cartflow_widget_arbitration.js`** logs `[CF ARBITRATION *]` open intents/decisions; **Exit Intent No-Cart v1** enforces **`exit_without_cart_blocked`** via **`gateExitIntentOpen()`** on exit open paths (other journeys remain shadow observe). Failure of one module aborts the chain (logged **`[CF V2 MODULE FAILED]`**). **Storefront Cart Bridge** (`cartflow_storefront_cart_bridge_*.js`) reads platform carts via adapters (Zid first: `/api/v1/cart`, add-to-cart response, `window.cart` fallback), validates a normalized payload, dedupes, and **only the core** posts **`POST /api/cart-event`** (`cart_state_sync`) with additive **`cf_storefront_cart_bridge`** metadata. The platform-neutral **Cart Event Bridge** (`cartflow_cart_event_bridge.js`) + signal adapters (`cartflow_cart_sources.js`) still normalize platform cart **signals** into one `CartFlowCartEvent`, route them through **`Cf.Triggers.onNormalizedCartEvent`** (orchestrator decides display), and delegate persistence to **Storefront Cart Bridge** before legacy **`cartflowSyncCartState`**. Canonical merchant store resolved server-side + `canonical_store_slug` from **`public-config`**. |
| **Complexity / bundle** | V2 split across **~10** smaller files (~**118 KB** source on disk, pre-minify); legacy monolith ~**337 KB**. Default path avoids legacy download; total widget surface still **multiple HTTP round-trips** for V2 (shim + tracker + loader + 9 modules). |
| **Duplication / coupling** | **Dual** reason APIs (**`/api/cartflow/reason`** vs **`/api/cart-recovery/reason`**); **dual** exit-intent implementations (V2 modules vs legacy file); **shared** backend contract (**`exit_intent_*`**, templates). **Operational / static** tests still scan **`cartflow_widget.js`** for parity. |
| **Legacy isolation** | V2 **does not** inject legacy at runtime (**`cartflow_widget_flows.js`** / audit: no `injectLegacyCartflowWidget`). Rollback is **merchant opt-in** + dev harness only. |
| **Risk level** | **Moderate:** default is healthy (V2), but **two** storefront stacks and **serial** multi-file load remain **maintainability and performance** considerations until legacy sunset. |

### 2.2 Dashboard UI

| Path / files | Purpose |
|--------------|---------|
| `GET /dashboard` | `merchant_app.html` + **`static/merchant_pe_v2.css`** — **Product Excellence V2 presentation** on production dashboard. **Home (`#home`):** `#ma-home-experience-root` — **Executive Control Center (Dashboard V3):** Executive Hero → Quick Metrics (4) → Attention Center → Knowledge Layer (Observation→Evidence→Explanation→Recommendation→Confidence) → Performance Summary → Activity Timeline (`static/merchant_dashboard_home_v1.js` + `.css` `ma-ecc-*`; live summary KPIs + `merchant_home_experience_v1`; no fake metrics). Global page hero hidden on overview. Fallback: Merchant Pulse V1 UI when ECC unavailable and `CARTFLOW_MERCHANT_PULSE_UI_V1=1`; else V2 Home Experience (`merchant_home_experience.js`). Backend Pulse attach remains `CARTFLOW_MERCHANT_PULSE_V1`. **Diagnostics & Testing:** Settings → `#settings-diagnostics` (legacy `#home-test-tools` redirects). **Carts Experience:** fills shared `#ma-page-hero-global.ma-vi-hero` (attention question + Commerce Language count story). **Carts (`#carts`):** work queue `#ma-carts-queue-v2` + desktop conversation `#ma-carts-panel-v2` + mobile CTA; guided story from `merchant_explanation_v1` / `cart_detail_projection_v1` (`merchant_dashboard_lazy.js`); **Cart Page V2 Phase 2.6** — `CartPageRenderingStateController` sole merchant-visible composition owner (Verdict/MI/Pending/Empty/Stories paint-only); **Phase 2** — Attention Verdict feeds shared Hero story (inline `#ma-carts-attention-verdict-v1` quiet; desktop queue column widened past PE 360px track); **Phase 1** — one primary CTA from `cart_page_primary_action_v1` (`data-cf-primary-action`; Archive demoted secondary); MI story cards (`merchant_intelligence_carts_v1.js`) — **LGE V1 target first consumer** (lifecycle governance not yet implemented). Hidden `#ma-tbody-all-carts` sync for filters. Lazy JSON via `/api/dashboard/*`. **Store Setup (`#home-setup`)** — `#ma-setup-readiness-root` + `#ma-setup-experience-root` + `#ma-activation-root`. **الملخص العام (`#home-month`)** — KPI grid. **Archive:** `POST /api/dashboard/cart-lifecycle/archive` + `/reopen`. Doc: **`docs/product_excellence_implementation_v1.md`**. |
| `GET /dashboard/recovery-settings` | `recovery_settings.html` — delay, attempts, WhatsApp fields; **`GET`/`POST /api/recovery-settings`**. |
| `GET /dashboard#whatsapp` | `merchant_app.html` — **تجربة واتساب V3:** اختيار المسار (CartFlow / واتساب أعمالي)، بطاقة «المسار الحالي»، إعدادات متقدمة (merchant فقط). **`#whatsapp-connect`** — صفحة ربط تجارية (ليس تقنية). **`GET`/`POST /api/recovery-settings`**. |
| `GET /dashboard#plans` | `merchant_app.html` — **read-only plans comparison** (Starter/Growth/Pro features + SAR pricing; Growth = Most Popular); current plan summary; **`GET /api/merchant/plans-catalog`**. No upgrade/billing. |
| `GET /dashboard#settings` | `merchant_app.html` — store connection + general settings + **read-only current plan card** (`GET /api/merchant/subscription`). |
| `GET /dashboard#vip` | `merchant_app.html` — VIP preferences (enable, threshold, notify toggle, note) + existing VIP cart table; **`/api/recovery-settings`**. |
| `GET /dashboard/vip-cart-settings` | `vip_cart_settings.html` — **أولوية حقيقية:** `AbandonedCart.status=abandoned` و‎`coalesce(cart_value,0) >= Store.vip_cart_threshold` عند تعريف العتبة؛ بدون عتبة لا تُعرض قائمة VIP. **بيانات تجريبية** منفصلة (`interactive: false`). **إرسال يدوي** → **`POST /api/dashboard/vip-cart/{abandoned_cart_row_id}/merchant-alert`**. عتبة VIP عبر **`/api/recovery-settings`**. |
| `GET /dashboard/exit-intent-settings` | `exit_intent_settings.html` — exit intent copy; loads/saves via recovery settings API + `static/cartflow_dashboard_messages.js`. |
| `GET /dashboard/cart-recovery-messages` | `cart_recovery_messages.html` — recovery message templates. |
| `GET /dashboard/widget-customization` | `widget_customization.html` — widget appearance. |
| Shared chrome | `templates/partials/dashboard_sidebar.html`, `templates/partials/recovery_dashboard_styles.html`. |

### 2.3 Exit Intent UI

- **V2:** **`cartflow_widget_triggers.js`** / **`cartflow_widget_flows.js`** (orchestration) with shell UI modules; duplicate open guards (e.g. **`[CF TRIGGER BLOCKED]`** paths) live in layered code. **Fast-add race recovery v1:** storefront bridge POST → **`onStorefrontCartPersisted`**; deferred flush uses **`[CF TRIGGER DEFERRED REPLAY]`** (never silent drop when cart-event succeeds).
- **Legacy:** Implemented inside **`static/cartflow_widget.js`** when that file is the only widget bootstrap.

Server-side template control (**`exit_intent_*`** on **`Store`**): `services/store_template_control.py` merge through **`/api/recovery-settings`**.

### 2.4 Cart Recovery UI

- **Dashboard:** recovery settings + cart recovery messages pages above.
- **Widget (V2):** layered **Ui / Flows / Api** backed by **`/api/cartflow/*`** helpers above.
- **Widget (legacy):** reason capture, handoff, and preview in **`cartflow_widget.js`** (including **`/api/cart-recovery/reason`** where wired).

**How UI interacts with backend:** JSON `fetch` / XHR to FastAPI routes; dashboards use embedded scripts or `static/cartflow_dashboard_messages.js` for shared save/load patterns against **`/api/recovery-settings`**.

### 2.5 Brand / visual identity (official foundation v1)

| Asset | Role |
|--------|------|
| `branding/cartflow_brand_foundation_v1/` | **Official source of truth** — approved Visual Identity board: CF monogram logo, six-color green palette, Tajawal typography, process + dashboard icons, governance. Spec only until product UI migration. |
| `branding/cartflow_brand_system_v1.md` | Superseded historical spec (blue tokens) — do not use for new work. |
| `branding/_archive/logo_explorations/` | **Frozen** exploration archive (v1, v2, validation) — do not use in production. |

Product UI may still use legacy styling (landing green variants, widget purple `#6C5CE7`) until each surface is migrated per foundation guidelines.

---

## 3) Backend Layer

### 3.1 FastAPI structure

- **`main.py`** — Core app: mounts `static/`, registers routers, **`POST /api/cart-event`**, **`/api/recovery-settings`**, **`/api/conversion`**, webhooks, **`GET /dashboard`**, **demo / commerce sandbox** routes (see §3.2.1), recovery sequence orchestration.
- **`routes/cartflow.py`** — `APIRouter(prefix="/api/cartflow")`: analytics, ready, public-config, generate-whatsapp-message, reason, etc.
- **`routes/knowledge.py`** — `APIRouter(prefix="/api/knowledge")`: **`GET /report`** — read-only evidence-based store insights (Knowledge Layer v1; merchant auth; no writes). Enriches with claim evidence, producer metadata, decisions, **`knowledge_routing_v1`** (KL surface), **`knowledge_layer_projection_v1`** (`display_cards` for UI). **`GET /health`** — read-only Knowledge Layer health (`knowledge_health_v1.py`: coverage, confidence distribution, stale/missing inputs, diagnosis codes; product foundation bridge via `knowledge_product_metrics_v1.py` only). Metrics: honest purchase attribution (`knowledge_purchase_attribution_v1.py`); VIP isolated in `vip_evidence` bucket (`knowledge_metrics_v1.py`).
- **`routes/product_data.py`** — `APIRouter(prefix="/api/product-data")`: **`GET /health`** — read-only product data readiness (`services/product_data/product_data_health_v1.py`: payload coverage/name/id/variant rates, catalog flag, confidence, readiness classification; **additive** `payload_health`, `foundation_health` (`product_foundation_health_v1.py`: snapshot/catalog/hesitation/purchase mapping coverage from foundation tables), `identity_coverage` (`product_identity_coverage_v1.py`: lines capture rate, carts with/without lines, identity capture status); merchant auth; no writes). **Cart line snapshots v1:** immutable `cart_line_snapshots` rows from widget `lines[]` on `cart_state_sync` / `cart_abandoned` via `services/product_data/product_cart_snapshots_v1.py` + `product_data_line_snapshots_hook_v1.py` delegate in `main.py` (insert-only; dedup by content hash; no UI/API). **Catalog normalization v1:** mutable canonical `product_catalog_entries` via `product_catalog_v1.py` + `product_catalog_normalizer_v1.py` (identity tiers A–E; chained from same cart-event hook; reads snapshots / `lines[]` / `cf_product_catalog_json`; no UI). **Hesitation Mapping v1:** immutable `product_hesitation_mappings` (Product ↔ Reason links) via `product_hesitation_mapping_v1.py` + `product_hesitation_types_v1.py`; non-blocking `product_hesitation_hook_v1.py` delegate fired from the reason-capture write path (`routes/cart_recovery_reason.py`) — maps the captured `CartRecoveryReason` to canonical products present in the session (from cart line snapshots); insert-only, `dedup_hash` unique; read helpers only (`reasons_for_product`, `products_for_reason`, `mapping_count_for_store`); no intelligence/UI/API. **Purchase Mapping v1:** immutable `product_purchase_mappings` (Product ↔ Purchase links) via `product_purchase_mapping_v1.py` + `product_purchase_types_v1.py`; non-blocking `product_purchase_hook_v1.py` delegate fired from Purchase Truth `record_purchase` (`services/cartflow_purchase_truth.py`) — maps canonical session products when purchase is confirmed; insert-only, `dedup_hash` unique; read helpers only (`purchases_for_product`, `products_for_purchase`, `purchase_mapping_count`); no intelligence/UI/API. **Governance v1:** read-only growth/query-cost/archive-policy diagnostics via `product_foundation_governance_v1.py` + related modules; `GET /api/product-data/governance/health` (merchant auth); no writes, archive jobs, or behavior changes to capture layers.
- **`routes/cart_recovery_reason.py`** — `APIRouter(prefix="/api/cart-recovery")`: **`POST /reason`** (widget reason persistence).
- **`routes/ops.py`** — **`GET /ping`**, **`GET /config-check`**, **`GET /decision-check`**, **`GET /health`**, **`GET /health/scheduler`**, dev mock-cart / set-token utilities.
- **`routes/public.py`** — **`GET /`** (landing), **`GET /register`** (302 → `/signup`).
- **`routes/merchant_pages.py`** — dashboard **redirect** routes (Phase 1B) plus **shell/template** routes (Phase 1C): `GET /dashboard`, `/dashboard/analytics`, `/dashboard/exit-intent-settings`, `/dashboard/general-settings`, `/dashboard/test-widget`, and legacy redirects. **`GET /dashboard/normal-carts/operations`** remains on **`main.py`**.
- **`routes/dev_diagnostics.py`** — read-only **`GET /dev/*`** diagnostic routes (Phase 1D + 1E-A): route inventory, config/production-readiness reports, widget/store-identity/runtime truth, recovery/lifecycle/merchant-truth traces, **`GET /dev/snapshot-truth-diagnostics`** (alias-aware snapshot vs live-builder vs dashboard visibility), **`GET /dev/dashboard-builder-parity`** (full DB → live builder → snapshot builder → persisted snapshot → dashboard parity chain with `drop_stage` / `parity_status`; governance gate before visibility fixes), **`GET /dev/operational-metrics`** (Operational Metrics v1 — platform health read model: dashboard/scheduler/snapshot/archive/data growth/DB pressure + `overall_status`; bounded, no PII; **Dashboard Read Model Observability v1** adds `metrics.dashboard.read_observability` — real per-endpoint route p50/p90/p99, snapshot_read/hot_slice latency, read-path distribution, hot-slice degrade rates — and `metrics.dashboard.builder_coverage` — builder cycle/lag seconds, stores waiting/never-built, stores_built_per_tick — via `services/dashboard_read_observability_v1.py`), recovery-health, delay/attempts/unit verify, dashboard render test, recovery logs, test-widget identity trace, plus preview/timing-only routes (`/dev/run-flow`, `/dev/whatsapp-message-test`, `/dev/should-send-test`, `/dev/recovery-timing-test`, `/dev/recovery-duplicate-test`). Write/send/simulation/VIP/recovery-settings harness routes remain on **`main.py`**; **`_DEV_ROUTES_ALLOWED_WHEN_NOT_DEVELOPMENT`** middleware unchanged.
- **`routes/demo_panel.py`** — demo utilities.
- **`routes/merchant_auth.py`** — SaaS auth HTML: **`/login`**, **`/signup`**, **`/logout`**, **`/forgot-password`**, **`/reset-password`**; signed cookie session (`services/merchant_auth_http.py`); gate middleware on **`/dashboard*`** and **`/api/dashboard*`** (`ENV=development` demo bypass only).
- **`services/merchant_setup_unified_p0.py`** — **P0 unified setup:** one home card (`unified_p0`, `setup_mode`) — sandbox steps (account → test-widget → recovery → carts → verified) then unlocked production (store connect, WhatsApp, templates, live widget); composes **`evaluate_onboarding_readiness`** + **`merchant_activation_v1`** + **`merchant_onboarding_v1`** (no recovery/send changes). Daily KPIs hidden via **`ma-setup-mode`** until complete.
- **`services/merchant_onboarding_journey_v2.py`** — **Onboarding V2 UX:** 6-step activation checklist + progress bar + nav locks + readiness card (truth-derived checklist: widget, store, WhatsApp, recovery) + guided empty states on **`GET /api/dashboard/summary`** (`merchant_setup_experience.activation_journey_v2`); merchant SPA render in **`merchant_dashboard_lazy.js`** (no behavior engine changes). Hardening audit: **`docs/cartflow_onboarding_hardening_audit_v2.md`**, tests **`tests/test_merchant_onboarding_hardening_audit.py`**.
- **`services/merchant_onboarding_v1.py`** + **`merchant_setup_experience_v1`** + **`merchant_onboarding_store.py`** + **`merchant_store_connection_v1.py`** — guided onboarding (5 steps); Store resolved only from authenticated merchant session; **`/dashboard#settings`** store connection card (Zid OAuth when `ZID_CLIENT_*` configured, else «ميزة الربط قيد الإعداد»); **`GET /api/merchant/store-connection`** (+ zid connect / disconnect). After Zid OAuth link, **`services/zid_storefront_widget_install_v1`** records widget install status (Partner Custom Snippet — no per-store install API); **`POST /api/storefront/widget-seen`** + loader beacon for **`widget_last_seen_at`**.
- **`services/merchant_activation_v1.py`** + **`merchant_dashboard_home_stage_v1.py`** — scoped activation demo; adaptive home stages (`activation` / `activated` / `production`) on **`GET /api/dashboard/summary`** (`merchant_activation.home_stage`); landing CTAs **`/signup`**.
- **`services/store_identity_v1.py`** + **`store_identity_aliases`** table — **canonical Store identity layer:** maps CartFlow `zid_store_id`, Zid permalink/numeric/uuid, future Salla ids, dashboard slugs, widget `public-config` keys, and recovery_key prefixes to one **`Store`** row via **`resolve_store_row_by_identifier`** (used by **`recovery_store_lookup`**, widget public API, OAuth sync, widget cache keys). No latest-Store fallback. **Warm hot path is offline:** `sync_connected_platform_identities()` makes **no live Zid network calls by default** (`warm_live_platform_sync_enabled()` / `CARTFLOW_WARM_LIVE_PLATFORM_SYNC=1` to opt in) — a blocking per-store Zid API call during request-time warm previously hung phone-capture / dashboard endpoints under the `db_warm` lock. Aliases are still backfilled offline from `Store` columns (`identity_backfill` stage) and refreshed at OAuth callback time.
- **`services/widget_configuration_trust_v1.py`** — **Widget Configuration Trust Recovery v1:** RC1–RC7 validation, dashboard↔public-config parity, visibility diagnostics (`would_show_widget`, blockers), closure criteria; consumed by **`GET /api/admin/operations/widget-configuration-trust`** (admin JSON, no UI).
- **`services/storefront_runtime_truth_gate_v1.py`** — **storefront runtime truth gate:** after widget settings save, syncs aliases + warms cache, compares dashboard DB vs `public-config` vs last storefront beacon (`POST /api/storefront/widget-seen`); persists `widget_runtime_truth_status` on **`Store`**; Admin Operations alert **`widget_settings_mismatch`** when mismatch/unresolved.
- **`services/vip_dashboard_batch_v1.py`** — **VIP dashboard batch read v1:** `GET /api/dashboard/vip-carts` hot path — one VIP cart SELECT + bulk reasons + bulk recovery logs → pure `vip_dashboard_row_contract()` (zero DB in projection). Optional `?debug_perf=1` metadata. Settings/other surfaces still use **`_vip_priority_cart_alert_list()`**.

### 3.2 Routes (representative)

| Route | Module | Role |
|--------|--------|------|
| `GET`/`POST /login`, `/signup`, `GET /logout`, `/forgot-password`, `/reset-password` | `routes/merchant_auth.py` | Merchant account signup/login; PBKDF2 passwords; reset tokens via Resend (`RESEND_API_KEY`, `RESEND_FROM_EMAIL`) or dev log when `ENV=development` without key. |
| `POST /api/cart-event` | `main.py` | Cart events (`cart_abandoned`, conversion flags, etc.). Merchant test-widget contract (when `merchant_activation=1`): enforce authenticated `store_slug`, evaluate old lifecycle truth, auto-reset to fresh `session_id`/`cart_id`/`recovery_key` when identity is not reusable. |
| `GET` / `POST /api/recovery-settings` | `main.py` | Store recovery + template + widget + VIP threshold merge/persist. |
| `POST /api/conversion` | `main.py` | Marks session converted; stops recovery. |
| `POST /api/cart-recovery/reason` | `routes/cart_recovery_reason.py` | Upsert `CartRecoveryReason` (Layer D). |
| `GET /api/cartflow/*`, `POST /api/cartflow/*` | `routes/cartflow.py` | Readiness, mock messages, analytics. |
| `GET /api/dashboard/recovery-trend` | `main.py` | Dashboard chart data. |
| `GET /api/dashboard/vip-carts` | `main.py` + `services/vip_dashboard_batch_v1.py` | VIP tab JSON — batch load (carts + reasons + logs) then pure projection; bounded SQL (≤4 typical); `?debug_perf=1` for dev query/timing metadata. |
| `GET /api/dashboard/vip-cart/{cart_row_id}/manual-contact` | `main.py` | VIP تواصل يدوي مع العميل — قراءة فقط: `manual_contact_available` + `contact_href` أو سبب عدم التوفر (لا إرسال واتساب). |
| `POST /api/dashboard/vip-cart/{cart_row_id}/merchant-alert` | `main.py` | VIP لوحة: تنبيه واتساب للتاجر فقط (`build_vip_merchant_alert_body` + `try_send_vip_merchant_whatsapp_alert`؛ `store_whatsapp_number` ثم `whatsapp_support_url`). |
| `POST /api/carts/{id}/send` | `main.py` | إرسال يدوي للعميل على الصفحة الرئيسية للوحة (`send_whatsapp_message` Meta path) — **ليس مسار VIP**. |
| `POST /dev/create-vip-test-cart` | `main.py` | Seed حقيقي: `AbandonedCart` VIP + `CartRecoveryReason` جلسة `test_vip_session` بدون ودجت (مسموح في الإنتاج عبر قائمة `_DEV_ROUTES_ALLOWED_WHEN_NOT_DEVELOPMENT`). |
| `GET /dev/widget-test`, `/dev/widget-test/cart` | `main.py` | **DEV-only legacy monolith harness** — HTML loads **`/static/cartflow_widget.js`** directly (no **`widget_loader`**, no **`cartflow_widget_runtime`**). **`no_dev_in_production`**: **`404`** unless **`ENV=development`**; intentionally **not** in **`_DEV_ROUTES_ALLOWED_WHEN_NOT_DEVELOPMENT`**. **`/demo/store`** remains **layered V2**. |
| `GET /dev/cartflow-simulation-report` | `main.py` + `services/cartflow_simulation_report_v1.py` | **Dry-run multi-store recovery simulation** for isolated **`sim-store-*`** slugs only (`stores=10` default, up to `100` with `expanded=true`). Runs 11 scenarios/store (cart, reason, 2-msg template, schedules, simulated sends, reply, return, purchase, dashboard truth). No WhatsApp/Twilio; `cleanup=true` purges simulation rows. |
| `POST /webhook/zid` | `main.py` | Zid webhook → cart upsert + purchase truth ingest when order-paid detected (`zid_webhook_purchase_v2`). |
| `POST` / `GET /webhook/whatsapp` | `main.py` | Twilio / inbound hook stubs (`[WA REPLY]` logging). |
| `POST /webhook/whatsapp/status` | `routes/whatsapp_delivery_webhook.py` | Twilio status callbacks → `whatsapp_delivery_truth_v1` (`[WA DELIVERY EVENT]` / `[WA DELIVERY TRUTH]`); no recovery execution. |
| `GET` / `POST /webhooks/meta/whatsapp` | `routes/meta_whatsapp_webhook.py` + `services/meta_whatsapp_webhook_v1.py` | Meta Cloud API webhook verify (`hub.challenge` when `META_WEBHOOK_VERIFY_TOKEN` matches) + inbound event ingest (delivered/read/inbound message); in-memory diagnostics only — **no recovery execution**. |
| `GET /admin/whatsapp-webhook` | `routes/admin_operations.py` | Admin HTML — last Meta webhook payload, delivered/read/inbound diagnostics + raw JSON. |
| `GET /admin/api/whatsapp-webhook/diagnostics` | `routes/admin_operations.py` | Admin JSON for Meta webhook diagnostics (session auth). |
| `GET /admin/support-diagnostics` | `routes/admin_ops.py` | Admin JSON: `build_admin_support_diagnostics` — What/Why/Action for support (session/store/recovery_key). |
| `GET /admin/support-diagnostics/ui` | `routes/admin_ops.py` | Admin HTML session/recovery lookup; reached from the **Support Diagnostics** page (`/admin/diagnostics`). |
| `GET /admin/operations` | `routes/admin_operations.py` | **Executive overview v3.5 (Action First Mode)** — Store Action Center expanded cards are **action-first**: Root Cause → Recommended Action → Verification, with Impact / Affected Signals / investigation hints in collapsed **Technical Context**. Priority queue (v3.4), root cause grouping (v3.3), production truth (v3.2). Presentation-only — no detection changes. |
| `GET /admin/operations/issues` | `routes/admin_operations.py` | **Current Issues** — operational alerts re-expressed in business language (`_build_current_issues`), one card per kind with Impact/Affected/Owner/Suggested Action/Verification. |
| `GET /admin/diagnostics` | `routes/admin_operations.py` | **Support Diagnostics** (support-only) — Recovery Resume Health card + collapsible «تفاصيل تقنية (للدعم فقط)» panels lazy-loading the Investigation/Analytics partials via `GET /admin/operations/section/investigation` and `/section/analytics`; quick links to operational-health, support-diagnostics/ui, control. |
| `GET /admin/operations/section/widget-health` | `routes/admin_operations.py` + `widget_health_v1.py` | **Widget Health v1** (read-only), **UX V2 action-first**: lazy HTML partial on the operations overview — status summary → Current Widget Issues cards (13 kinds; Problem→Impact→Where→Suggested Action→Verification + collapsed Technical Details) shown first; full per-store matrix (installed, public-config, beacon, identity, cart bridge, hesitation armed, shown, last error, last seen, status 🟢/🟡/🔴) collapsed under «Store Diagnostics». UI-only filters: Store Type (real/test) + hide-healthy by default (logic in parent overview script). Parses beacon `runtime_truth.widget_health` additively; no truth-system duplication. |
| `GET /admin/operations/snapshot` | `routes/admin_operations.py` + `admin_operational_snapshot_v1.py` | Read-only JSON operational snapshot export (optional `?store_slug=`); admin session auth; no secrets. |
| `GET /api/admin/operations/pilot-foundation` | `routes/admin_operations.py` + `services/pilot_operational_foundation_v1.py` + `services/pilot_operational_foundation_mapping_v1.py` | **Pilot Operational Visibility v1** — read-only JSON composition (`primary_reason`, `action_required`, attention queue, pilot health overview, top issues); production stores in headline metrics; optional `?include_demo=1` sidecar; composes Store Action Center + onboarding reality + ops alerts only; no merchant/recovery behavior changes. Design: `docs/cartflow_pilot_operational_foundation_v1.md`. |
| `GET /api/admin/operations/widget-configuration-trust` | `routes/admin_operations.py` + `services/widget_configuration_trust_v1.py` | **Widget Configuration Trust Recovery v1** — RC validation, dashboard↔public-config parity, visibility diagnostics, closure criteria; admin JSON only. Report: `docs/cartflow_widget_configuration_trust_recovery_report_v1.md`. |
| `GET /admin/operations/recovery-resume-inspect` | `routes/admin_operations.py` + `admin_recovery_resume_inspect_scan_v1.py` | Read-only recovery resume inspect (filters: status, store_slug, resume_only, stale_only). |
| `GET /admin/operations/recovery-resume-scan` | same | Dry-run resume scan simulation — no DB writes or execution. |
| `GET /admin/operational-health` | `routes/admin_operations.py` | Deep operational control / risk cards (`services/admin_operational_health.py`). |
| `GET /health/scheduler` | `main.py` | Scheduler role + overdue/stale counts (same source as ops center scheduler card). |
| `GET /demo/store`, `/demo/store/cart`, `/demo/store/checkout`, `/demo/cart`, `/demo/cart/checkout`, `/demo/store/product/{id}` | `main.py` | **Commerce sandbox (default `store_slug=demo`):** multi-page catalog, cart, lightweight checkout. |
| `GET /demo/store2`, `/demo/store2/cart`, `/demo/store2/checkout`, `/demo/store2/product/{id}` | `main.py` | Same UI with **isolation** (`demo2` slug / `demo2_cart` localStorage) for recovery tests. |

### 3.2.1 Demo commerce sandbox (v1) — reference

**Purpose:** One in-app “realistic lightweight store” that exercises the **real** recovery pipeline (cart events, continuation, dashboard, offers/product intelligence when configured) without replacing production widget architecture.

| Piece | Location / behavior |
|--------|---------------------|
| **Catalog (data)** | **`services/demo_sandbox_catalog.py`** — `SANDBOX_PRODUCTS`, `SANDBOX_PRODUCT_ORDER`, PDP numbering (`SANDBOX_PRODUCT_KEY_BY_NUM`). Fields: `id`, `sku`, `name`, `price` / `unit_price`, `category`, **`normalized_category`**, **`product_family`** (per SKU), descriptions, `url` / `image` (picsum seeds), **`related_keys`**, **`cheaper_alternative_keys`**, **`available`**. **Rule-first only** (no AI): relationships are explicit lists on each SKU. |
| **URLs per store** | `product_demo_url(nav_base, key)` — `/demo/store/...` vs `/demo/store2/...` so `demo2` PDP links stay isolated. |
| **Merchant sync** | `merchant_catalog_for_intelligence_sync()` / `merchant_catalog_json_string()` — JSON shaped for **`product_catalog`** in **`/api/recovery-settings`** (paste in dashboard **العروض الذكية** so intelligence and offers match real catalog rows). Rows may include **`normalized_category`** and **`product_family`** for cheaper-matching (see **`cartflow_product_intelligence.py`**). Template context: `demo_merchant_catalog_json`. |
| **Store UI** | **`templates/demo_store.html`** — grid from `demo_grid_rows`, `window.CF_DEMO_PRODUCTS` + `window.CF_DEMO_NAV_BASE` from server JSON; PDP with image + related links; cart **subtotal** + link to checkout; **checkout** page with **COD** button → **`window.cartflowTriggerDemoConversion`** → **`POST /api/conversion`** (`purchase_completed: true`), then local cart clear + client converted flag (same as demo panel). |
| **Demo panel** | **`static/cartflow_demo_panel.js`** — cart page only UI; **`cartflowStartDemoScenario`** seeds **`hp_pro`** first (premium headphones) to surface **cheaper-alternative** scenarios; **`cartflowTriggerDemoConversion`** exported for checkout page. |
| **Abandon payload shape** | Demo sends **`cart` as a JSON array** of line objects (`id`, `name`, `price`, `category`, …). **`services/recovery_product_context.py`** `_first_line_items_list` accepts **`cart` as list** so product context / intelligence see line items. |
| **Lab Reset (P1)** | **`services/demo_lab_reset_v1.py`** — authoritative demo-only reset for Commerce Lab (`store_slug=demo` only). Fixed identity `s_lab_v1_s1` / `cf_cart_lab_v1_s1` / recovery_key `demo:cf_cart_lab_v1_s1` (stable cart). Lab customer phone `966511114449` (not `CARTFLOW_DEMO_TEST_PHONE`, which production treats as merchant-equal). Clears carts/recoveries/purchases/timelines/schedules/movement/temp Lab memory; preserves Store + catalog. Rejects non-demo / `merchant_activation`. Idempotent. Tests: `tests/test_demo_lab_reset_v1.py`. |
| **Scenario 1 runner (P2)** | **`services/demo_lab_scenario1_v1.py`** + CLI `scripts/_demo_lab_v1_scenario1.py` — Visit→PDP→add→leave→recovery→return→purchase on `hp_pro` @ 449. Always Lab-Resets first. Production paths only (`/demo/store*`, `/api/cart-event`, `/api/cartflow/reason`, `/api/conversion`, Signals, Pulse). Structured PASS/FAIL report. No UI. Tests: `tests/test_demo_lab_scenario1_v1.py`. |
| **Tests** | `tests/test_demo_behavioral_navigation.py` (routes, checkout), `tests/test_cart_recovery_sequence_behavior.py`, `tests/test_recovery_product_context.py` (list-cart case), `tests/test_demo_lab_reset_v1.py`, `tests/test_demo_lab_scenario1_v1.py`. |

**Do not use the sandbox as:** a second application or a bypass of lifecycle, continuation, or dashboard settings — it is wired to the same APIs and session keys as the existing demo.

### 3.3 Services (`services/`)

| Area | Modules |
|------|---------|
| WhatsApp mode (Production Strategy P1 + Mode Selection V1) | `merchant_whatsapp_mode_v1.py`, `admin_whatsapp_visibility_v1.py` — `stores.whatsapp_mode` (`cartflow_managed` default / `merchant_whatsapp`); prominent Arabic mode cards on `#whatsapp`; Path B panel (Meta pairing + Embedded Signup + `#whatsapp-connect`); admin `/admin/whatsapp`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_mode_v1.py`. |
| WhatsApp Dual Architecture V1 (design) | **Path A** `cartflow_managed` (CartFlow Shared WhatsApp) vs **Path B** `merchant_whatsapp` (Merchant-Owned) — independent readiness, diagnostics, onboarding, sending provider (adapter boundary), dashboard messaging; path switch preserves settings; recovery engine unchanged. Target modules: `whatsapp_dual_readiness_v1`, `whatsapp_path_router_v1`, path A/B presentation builders. Doc: `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_dual_architecture_v1.md`. |
| WhatsApp Embedded Signup Foundation V1 | Path B one-click onboarding prep — readiness states (`not_started` / `pairing_required` / `connected` / `failed`); `merchant_whatsapp_embedded_signup_readiness_v1.py`; placeholder `#whatsapp-connect` + `/dashboard/whatsapp-connect`; read-only `whatsapp_embedded_signup` API block. No SDK/token exchange/send/recovery changes. Doc: `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_embedded_signup_foundation_v1.md`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_embedded_signup_readiness_v1.py`. |
| WhatsApp template registry (Production Strategy P2) | `merchant_whatsapp_template_registry_v1.py`, `merchant_whatsapp_reason_mapping_v1.py`, `merchant_whatsapp_template_layer_v1.py`, `admin_whatsapp_template_visibility_v1.py` — canonical 11-key registry + locked reason→template map; merchant edits content on `#trigger-templates` only; admin `GET /api/admin/whatsapp/templates` + `/store-templates`. Doc: `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_production_strategy_phase2_template_registry_reason_mapping_foundation_audit_v1.md`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_template_registry_v1.py`. |
| WhatsApp template execution policy (Production Strategy P3) | `merchant_whatsapp_template_execution_policy_v1.py` — read-only 3-stage execution model, stop/skip vocabulary, VIP lane rules, Managed sender internal controls; `GET /api/admin/whatsapp/execution-policy`. No send/runtime/Meta migration. Doc: `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_production_strategy_phase3_template_execution_policy_audit_v1.md`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_template_execution_policy_v1.py`. |
| WhatsApp template library & guardrails (Production Strategy P4) | `merchant_whatsapp_template_library_v1.py`, `merchant_whatsapp_meta_policy_awareness_v1.py`, `merchant_whatsapp_timing_guardrails_v1.py`, `admin_whatsapp_template_library_visibility_v1.py` — versioned library, approval/fallback architecture, calm guidance, stage 2/3 timing clamps on trigger-template save; `GET /api/admin/whatsapp/template-library`. No Meta/send migration. Doc: `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_production_strategy_phase4_template_library_meta_readiness_policy_guardrails_audit_v1.md`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_template_library_phase4_v1.py`. |
| WhatsApp connection & readiness (Production Strategy P5) | `merchant_whatsapp_connection_readiness_v1.py`, enriched `merchant_whatsapp_readiness_ui.py` — canonical connection states, readiness dimensions, production-truth copy; merchant `#whatsapp` readiness card; admin `GET /api/admin/whatsapp/connection-readiness` (per-store includes `readiness_diagnostic_temp`). No Meta/send migration. **UX V2 (action-first):** `CONNECTION_STATE_ACTION_FIRST` + `build_action_first_card` drive a per-state title/next-action/single-CTA/outcome card (`action_first` in merchant API); engine/states/truth unchanged. **Merchant presentation V1/V2:** `merchant_whatsapp_readiness_presentation_v1.py` — completed journey shows «تم إكمال إعداد واتساب» + separate «حالة الإرسال» (Meta Business Platform pairing CTA when production send not ready; «قيد التجهيز بواسطة CartFlow» only for sandbox/ops gaps); strips diagnostic from merchant API. **Onboarding Journeys UI V1:** `merchant_whatsapp_onboarding_journeys_v1.py` — `stores.whatsapp_onboarding_journey` (4 merchant paths); journey selector + guidance on `#whatsapp`; CTA «اختيار مسار واتساب» / «متابعة التفعيل» (in-progress only); completed → «تعديل إعدادات واتساب». **Journey Execution Layer V1:** `merchant_whatsapp_journey_execution_v1.py` — journey-specific actionable CTAs + `whatsapp_onboarding_journey_status` (`not_started`/`in_progress`/`completed`); progress UI; readiness/admin integration; reserved future Meta hooks (not implemented). Doc: `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_production_reality_phase1_journey_execution_layer_v1.md`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_journey_execution_v1.py`, `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_readiness_final_merchant_ux_v1.py`. Doc: `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_onboarding_journeys_ui_v1.md`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_onboarding_journeys_v1.py`. Doc: `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_production_strategy_phase5_merchant_connection_architecture_readiness_audit_v1.md`.
