Tests: `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_connection_readiness_v1.py`, `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_readiness_ux_v2.py`. |
| WhatsApp send / gates | `whatsapp_send.py` (`send_whatsapp`, `should_send_whatsapp`), `whatsapp_recovery.py`, `whatsapp_queue.py` |
| Meta WhatsApp webhook (v1) | `meta_whatsapp_webhook_v1.py` — Cloud API verify + event parse (delivered/read/inbound); in-memory diagnostics; admin `/admin/whatsapp-webhook`. Tests: `tests/test_meta_whatsapp_webhook_v1.py`. No recovery hook. |
| WhatsApp delivery truth (v1) | `whatsapp_delivery_truth_v1.py` — `DeliveryTruth`, status webhook ingest, `whatsapp_delivery_truth` table; `queued` ≠ delivered; attribution hook reserved (`customer_delivered_for_attribution_future`). See `docs/whatsapp_delivery_truth_v1.md`. |
| WhatsApp production reality (v2) | `whatsapp_production_reality_v2.py` — 24h window (`inside_24h` / `outside_24h` / `unknown`), `[WA WINDOW CHECK]` / `[WA TEMPLATE DECISION]`; production send gate `[WA TEMPLATE ENFORCEMENT]` on `send_whatsapp` when `recovery_uses_real_whatsapp()`. See `docs/whatsapp_production_reality_v2.md`, `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_template_24h_enforcement_audit_v1.md`. **Definitive launch model (decision only):** `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_production_reality_v1.md` — Day 1 CartFlow Managed + Meta Cloud API; Phase 2 Merchant WABA via Embedded Signup; provider-layer boundary. **Phase 1 architecture audit:** `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_production_reality_phase1_architecture_audit_v1.md`. **Phase 1.5 sender strategy:** `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_production_reality_phase1_5_production_sender_strategy_audit_v1.md` — Meta Cloud API primary. **Phase 2.0 Meta readiness audit:** `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_production_reality_phase2_0_meta_production_readiness_audit_v1.md` — gap analysis; ops phases 2.1–2.3 before code 2.4. **Template library foundation audit:** `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_template_library_foundation_audit_v1.md` — frozen 8-key library (`VIP_ALERT`, `PRICE`, `SHIPPING`, `QUALITY`, `DELIVERY`, `WARRANTY`, `CONTINUATION`, `RECOVERY_REMINDER`), message classes (`customer_message`, `merchant_alert`, `operational_alert`), delivery lifecycle, CartFlow-owned approval / merchant variables only. |
| Merchant onboarding reality (v1) | `merchant_onboarding_reality_v1.py` — `[MERCHANT READINESS]` dimensions + admin «جاهزية المتجر»; audit `docs/audit_merchant_onboarding_reality_v1.md`. |
| SaaS plans / subscription (Phase 1) | `cartflow_plans_v1.py`, `cartflow_entitlements_v1.py`, `merchant_subscription_v1.py`, `schema_merchant_subscription.py` — canonical Starter/Growth/Pro entitlements; `MerchantUser.current_plan` + `plan_status` + `plan_source` + dates; `has_feature()` / `is_starter()` / `is_growth()` / `is_pro()` (enforcement off by default); `GET /api/merchant/subscription`; marketplace event stubs (`zid_plan_*`, `salla_plan_*`). Audit: `docs/cartflow_saas_foundation_phase1_marketplace_plan_system_audit_v1.md`. |
| SaaS plans UI (Phase 2) | `merchant_plans_catalog_v1.py` — approved SAR pricing + marketing feature lists; `GET /api/merchant/plans-catalog`; `static/merchant_plans_ui.js` + `#plans` page + settings current-plan card; visual proof `scripts/_saas_plans_ui_out/`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_plans_ui_v1.py`. |
| SaaS admin subscription (Phase 3) | `admin_subscription_control_v1.py` — admin trial/plan assignment, `merchant_subscription_audit_logs`, `GET /admin/subscriptions/control`, `POST /api/admin/subscriptions/{id}/action`; trial fields on `MerchantUser`; `subscription_entitlements_blocked()` when enforcement on. Doc: `docs/cartflow_saas_foundation_phase3_trial_admin_subscription_control_audit_v1.md`. Tests: `tests/test_admin_subscription_control_v1.py`. |
| SaaS billing interval (Phase 3.1) | `merchant_billing_interval_v1.py` — `billing_interval` on `MerchantUser`; auto date rules for trial/monthly/annual/custom; admin actions `activate_monthly` / `activate_annual` / `activate_custom`; audit columns for interval + start dates; `GET /api/merchant/subscription` exposes interval + display expiry. Doc: `docs/cartflow_saas_foundation_phase3_1_automatic_subscription_dates_audit_v1.md`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_billing_interval_v1.py`. |
| Marketplace subscription sync (v1 audit) | Architecture-only — six marketplace events (`zid_plan_*`, `salla_plan_*` incl. cancelled); normalized adapter → `MerchantUser` mapping; idempotent receipts + audit; admin fallback; failure cases. Doc: `docs/cartflow_marketplace_subscription_sync_v1_audit.md`. No webhook implementation yet. |
| SaaS subscription experience (Phase 4) | `merchant_subscription_experience_v1.py` — days remaining, health messages, plan benefits, upgrade discovery; enriched `GET /api/merchant/subscription`; Status Card V2 on `#settings` / `#plans`; admin list days + health. Doc: `docs/cartflow_saas_foundation_phase4_subscription_experience_audit_v1.md`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_subscription_experience_v1.py`. |
| Merchant production readiness path (v1) | `merchant_production_readiness_path_v1.py` — score 0–100, missing items, `[MERCHANT NEXT ACTION]`, progression card; `docs/merchant_production_readiness_path_v1.md`. |
| Readiness ownership path (v1) | `readiness_ownership_path_v1.py` — owner per blocker (`merchant` / `cartflow_ops` / `provider` / `platform` / `shared`); `[READINESS OWNER]`; admin card المشكلة/المسؤول/الإجراء/الأثر. |
| Delays | `recovery_delay.py` (`get_recovery_delay` per tag), timing also in `whatsapp_send.recovery_delay_to_seconds` from `Store` |
| Multi-message | `recovery_multi_message.py` (`multi_message_slots_for_abandon`) |
| Reason templates | `reason_template_recovery.py`, `store_reason_templates.py`, `recovery_message_templates.py` |
| Decision | `decision_engine.py` (Layer D.2 message/action); `main` imports `decide_recovery_action` via `decision_engine.py` shim |
| VIP | `vip_cart.py` (`is_vip_cart`, `merchant_vip_threshold_int`, `vip_operational_lane_diagnostics`, `abandoned_cart_in_vip_operational_lane`), `vip_merchant_alert.py` (merchant-only Twilio alert + `resolve_vip_alert_destination`), `vip_operational_truth_v1.py` (lane isolation + delivery poll + VIP log statuses) |
| Session phone | `recovery_session_phone.py` |
| Store JSON fields | `store_trigger_templates.py`, `store_template_control.py`, `store_widget_customization.py` |
| AI / copy | `ai_message_builder.py` |
| Demo commerce catalog | `demo_sandbox_catalog.py` — static SKUs, grid/JS maps, merchant `product_catalog` export (§3.2.1). |
| Demo Commerce Lab Reset (P1) | `demo_lab_reset_v1.py` — demo-only idempotent Lab Reset; fixed Lab identity; preserves catalog (§3.2.1). |
| Demo Commerce Lab Scenario 1 (P2) | `demo_lab_scenario1_v1.py` — Visit→…→Purchase runner on `hp_pro` @ 449; Signals + Pulse asserts (§3.2.1). |
| Product context from cart | `recovery_product_context.py` — infers cheaper alternative from line items; supports **`cart` as list** for demo payloads. |
| Cheaper-product matching (continuation only) | `cartflow_product_intelligence.py` — normalized category / type signals, **`cheaper_candidate_score`**, strict lower-price + availability, structured logs (`[ALTERNATIVE REJECTED]`, `[ALTERNATIVE SCORE]`, `[FALLBACK USED]`); catalog normalization in **`cartflow_merchant_offer_settings.normalize_product_catalog`**. |
| Operational controls (kill switches) | `operational_control_v1.py` — pause WA / new scheduling / store / reason / continuation / provider; gates before `whatsapp_send`, new `RecoverySchedule` rows, continuation. **Fail-closed v1:** when durable OC state cannot be loaded, gates block (no silent bypass). **Durable v1:** singleton `OperationalControlSnapshot` (`operational_control_snapshots`, id=1) via `operational_control_store_v1.py` + `schema_operational_control.py`; in-process cache reloads from DB before gate reads (shared across workers, survives restart). Admin UI/API: `/admin/control`, `GET /api/admin/operational-control/state`, **`GET /api/admin/operational-health`** (Operational Truth Center JSON + **`integrations`** block from `integration_health_v1.py`). |
| Provider send timeout (v1) | `provider_send_timeout_v1.py` — hard ceiling on Twilio `messages.create` via `ThreadPoolExecutor` + `TwilioHttpClient` timeout (`PROVIDER_SEND_TIMEOUT_SECONDS`, default 30s); logs `[PROVIDER TIMEOUT]` / `[PROVIDER FAILURE]`; returns `provider_timeout` → `whatsapp_failed`; ring buffer `drain_recent_provider_send_events()` surfaced in `cartflow_runtime_health` `provider_runtime`. Wired in `whatsapp_send.send_whatsapp` only (all recovery/VIP paths use this). |
| Request hang diagnostics (v1) | `request_hang_diag_v1.py`, `demo_store_request_diag_v1.py`, `dashboard_refresh_state_guard_v1.py` — always-on stage logs `[DEMO STORE STAGE]` / `[REFRESH STATE STAGE]` with `trace_id` + `elapsed_ms`; refresh-state wall guard (`CARTFLOW_REFRESH_STATE_WALL_BUDGET_S`, default 4.5s) returns safe partial token instead of hanging; `[REFRESH STATE DEADLINE EXCEEDED]`. Observability only — no widget/recovery/classification changes. |
| DB Ready deep trace (v1, Step 4A) | `db_ready_diag_v1.py`, `db_ready_operational_snapshot_v1.py`, `db_ready_admin_v1.py` — `[DB READY STAGE]` / `[DB READY LOCK]` on `_merchant_dashboard_db_ready()` + `_ensure_cartflow_api_db_warmed()` + `ensure_production_store_schema()` branches; per-stage `query_count` + `total_sql_ms`; durable singleton `DbReadyOperationalSnapshot`; Admin Operations lazy section **Dashboard Initialization (Request Health)** with healthy/slow/blocking thresholds (3s / 15s). Observability only — no optimization. |
| DB Ready query explosion isolation (v1, Step 4B.1) | Extends Step 4A: `[DB READY SUBSTAGE]` per internal schema helper (widget_schema column migrations, merchant_auth bootstrap, widget_install columns, identity backfill/sync, schema verifiers); `[DB READY TOP STAGES]` ranked by query count; snapshot `top_substages_json` + Admin panel sub-stage table. Diagnostics only. |
| DB Ready root-cause classification (v1, Step 4B.2) | `db_ready_stage_reason_v1.py` — read-only probes emit `reason=` on tracked stages (`widget_schema`, `identity_backfill`, `identity_backfill_register`, `production_schema`, `bootstrap_merchant_auth`); identity backfill row counters (`rows_scanned`, `rows_updated`, `rows_inserted`); snapshot `stage_classifications_json` + Admin **Why did this run?** table. Diagnostics only — no optimization. |
| DB Ready startup warm (v1, Step 4B.3) | `db_ready_startup_warm_v1.py` — non-blocking background `_ensure_cartflow_api_db_warmed(trace_source="startup")` at app startup; `[DB READY STARTUP WARM]` logs; refresh-state defers with partial token while warm runs; snapshot startup warm status + Admin **Startup warm** panel. Moves cold-start cost off user-facing requests when warm completes first. |
| DB Ready restart survival (v1, Step 4B.4–4B.5) | `db_ready_restart_survival_v1.py` — durable restart verification (protection-focused PASS/FAIL, timing classification, `used_safe_path`); `[RESTART SURVIVAL]` logs with `timing=` / `protected=` / `reason=`; Admin **Restart Survival Verification** card; alert `dashboard_restart_survival_failed`. Read-only — no warm/behavior changes. |

### 3.4 Database models

Defined in **`models.py`**; optional columns ensured at runtime via **`schema_widget.ensure_store_widget_schema`**.

---

## 4) Core Logic Layer (Hard-core)

### 4.1 Detection Logic (Layer B)

- **`config_system.py`** — `get_cartflow_config(store_slug=...)`: isolated defaults (`recovery_delay_minutes`, `max_recovery_attempts`, `whatsapp_recovery_enabled`, etc.). Documented in code as **Layer B** (no DB required).
- **`services/whatsapp_send.py`** — `_recovery_config(store)` merges Layer B with store slug via `get_cartflow_config` for delay / attempt gates inside **`should_send_whatsapp`**.

### 4.2 Reason Capture (Layer C / D)

- **Layer D (persistence)** — **`POST /api/cart-recovery/reason`** in `routes/cart_recovery_reason.py`: validates payload, upserts **`CartRecoveryReason`** (`store_slug`, `session_id`, `reason`, `sub_category`, `custom_text`, `customer_phone`, `user_rejected_help`, etc.).
- Widget stores session keys and posts **`reason_tag`** aligned with dashboard / templates (see layered sources and comments in **`cartflow_widget.js`**).

### 4.3 Persistence (Layer D)

- **`CartRecoveryReason`** — last reason per `(store_slug, session_id)`; drives `updated_at` / last activity for delay checks.
- **`CartRecoveryLog`** — append-only recovery attempts (`status`, `step`, `message`, …); includes **`vip_manual_handling`** for VIP dashboard lines.
- **`RecoverySchedule`** — durable delayed-recovery jobs (`recovery_key`, `due_at`, `effective_delay_seconds`, `delay_source`, `context_json`); survives process restart; resumed on startup via **`services/recovery_restart_survival`**.
- **`AbandonedCart`** — `zid_cart_id`, `cart_value`, `vip_mode`, etc.; VIP threshold comparison uses **`_abandoned_cart_cart_value_for_recovery`** in `main.py`.
- **`Store`** — recovery delays, units, attempts, templates, `vip_cart_threshold`, WhatsApp fields.
- **`schema_widget.py`** — idempotent `ALTER TABLE` helpers so ORM matches SQLite/Postgres deployments.

### 4.4 Decision Engine (D.2)

- **`services/decision_engine.py`** — `decide_recovery_action(reason_tag, store=..., is_vip_cart_flag=False)`:
  - **Normal:** maps reason → `action` + message via **`resolve_whatsapp_recovery_template_message`**؛ يُعاد أيضاً **`send_customer: true`** و **`send_merchant: false`**.
  - **VIP (`is_vip_cart_flag=True`):** قبل أي منطق قوالب — يُعاد **`action: vip_manual_handling`**, **`message: ""`**, **`send_customer: false`**, **`send_merchant: true`** مع سجل **`[VIP OVERRIDE ACTIVATED]`**, **`[VIP FLOW STOPPED]`**, **`[VIP CUSTOMER BLOCKED]`**.
- **`main._vip_recovery_decision_layer(reason_tag, store)`** يستدعي المحرك مع **`is_vip_cart_flag=True`** عند مسارات VIP في `main.py`.
- **Production recovery text** إلى العميل يمر غالباً بـ **`reason_template_recovery.resolve_recovery_whatsapp_message_with_reason_templates`** داخل **`main._run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned_impl`**؛ مسار VIP يوقف ذلك قبل الإرسال.

### 4.5 WhatsApp Integration (D.3)

- **Customer recovery (Twilio):** **`send_whatsapp`** in `services/whatsapp_send.py` — called from **`main._run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned_impl`** after gates. Logs **`[WA SEND PATH]`**, **`[WA SENT]`**, **`[WA STATUS]`** when trace/env allows.
- **Customer manual / CTA:** **`send_whatsapp_message`** in `main.py` — Meta Graph interactive `cta_url` (**`/api/carts/{id}/send`**).
- **Gates:** **`_blocked_send_whatsapp_if_user_rejected_help`** prints **`[BLOCK WA - USER REJECTED HELP]`**; **`should_send_whatsapp`** implements quiet period vs `CartRecoveryReason.updated_at`.

### 4.6 Delay Logic

1. **`handle_cart_abandoned`** claims session (`_try_claim_recovery_session`), loads store, **VIP short-circuit** (see §4.9), else may schedule **multi** or async **`_run_recovery_dispatch_cart_abandoned`**.
2. **`_run_recovery_dispatch_cart_abandoned_impl`** polls **`_reason_tag_for_session`**, then either **`_schedule_recovery_multi_slots`** or computes **`get_recovery_delay`** (`services/recovery_delay.py`) vs elapsed time, then **`asyncio.create_task(_run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned(..., delay_seconds=remain))`**.
3. **`_run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned_impl`**: **فحص VIP قبل **`asyncio.sleep`**** (خرج بدون إرسال عميل ولا انتظار)، ثم **`await asyncio.sleep(delay_seconds)`** → dedupe → conversion / user-rejected → **فحص VIP ثانٍ** دفاعيًا → القوالب و**`should_send_whatsapp`** و**`send_whatsapp`** للعميل حسب المسارات غير المحظورة.

Print-style trace: **`[DELAY STARTED]`**, **`[DELAY WAITING]`**, **`[DELAY FINISHED]`**, **`[CARTFLOW DELAY CHECK]`**, **`[DELAY BLOCKED]`**, **`[DELAY CONFIG]`** (from `whatsapp_send`).

### 4.7 Multi-message logic

- **`services/recovery_multi_message.multi_message_slots_for_abandon(reason_tag, store)`** — reads **`Store.reason_templates_json`**; if enabled and multiple messages → list of `{index, delay_seconds, text}`.
- **`main._schedule_recovery_multi_slots`** — one asyncio task per slot, each calling **`_run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned`** with **`multi_slot_index`** / **`multi_message_text`**.
- Logs: **`[MULTI MESSAGE MODE ACTIVATED]`**, **`[MULTI MESSAGE SCHEDULED]`**, **`[MULTI WA SEND ATTEMPT]`**, **`[MULTI WA SEND RESULT]`**, **`[MULTI MESSAGE SENT]`**, **`[MULTI MESSAGE FAILED]`**, **`[RECOVERY FULLY COMPLETED]`**.

### 4.8 Per-reason system

- **`get_recovery_delay(reason_tag, store_config)`** — per-tag default seconds in `services/recovery_delay.py` (extendable via `store_config.recovery_delays` if passed).
- **Reason templates** — `reason_templates_json` + `reason_template_recovery` / `store_reason_templates` / `recovery_message_templates` control message body and whether WhatsApp is blocked for a reason.

### 4.9 VIP handling

- **Threshold:** **`Store.vip_cart_threshold`** (null → VIP ignored); مجموع السلة من **`_abandoned_cart_cart_value_for_recovery`** / الحمولة مقابل **`services/vip_cart.is_vip_cart(cart_total, store)`**. **`cart_value`** مفقود → لا اعتبار VIP في الإشارة الأولى؛ يمكن للمهام اللاحقة إعادة التقييم.
- **لوحة السلال — مسار واحد:** **`/dashboard/normal-carts`** يستبعد السلال حيث `cart_value >= vip_cart_threshold`؛ **`/dashboard/vip-cart-settings`** يعرضها فقط عند وجود عتبة صالحة. **`GET /api/dashboard/normal-carts`** يضمّ صفوف **`AbandonedCart`** المرتبطة بسجلات **`sent_real`/`mock_sent`** حتى لو خارج حد **`last_seen_at`**، ويُبقي مجموعات «مُرسل» في تبويب السلال النشطة حتى نتيجة نهائية (شراء / إيقاف / اكتمال تسلسل). **ملكية الحقيقة (Phase 2):** `customer_lifecycle_state` (من `services/customer_lifecycle_states_v1`) هو المصدر الوحيد لشارة الحالة، bucket التبويب، العدّادات، وتموضع الأرشفة؛ `merchant_cart_row_classifier` يبقى طبقة مشتقة/توافق غير سلطوية، وtimeline دليل فقط. **LT-C1 CI-enforced (v1):** `customer_lifecycle_state` / `CustomerLifecycleStateV1` may only be *minted* by `services/customer_lifecycle_states_v1.py`; all other modules read/propagate only. Gate `scripts/lifecycle_truth_enforcement_v1.py` (+ `.github/workflows/lifecycle_truth_gate.yml`, `tests/test_lifecycle_truth_enforcement_v1.py`) fails the build on any lifecycle mint/duplicate-classifier outside LT-C1 — see `docs/lifecycle_truth_enforcement_v1.md`. **Cart archive identity (V1):** `services/cart_action_identity_v1.py` — archive/reopen mutations use cart-specific keys only; `store_slug:session_id` session-only alias excluded from writes and from `merchant_archived` read on lifecycle attach. **Cart reopen semantics (V1 decision):** `docs/cartflow_cart_reopen_semantics_v1.md` — reopen = restore active merchant visibility, not recovery restart; forbidden for purchased truth. Doc: `docs/cartflow_cart_action_audit_v1.md`. التشخيص في JSON البطاقة: `cart_total`, `vip_threshold`, `is_vip_cart`, `operational_lane` (`normal` \| `vip`). **`vip_mode`** في DB يبقى للمزامنة/الاسترجاع؛ العرض والـ **`POST …/merchant-alert`** و**`…/lifecycle`** يعتمدون **`is_vip_cart`** على العتبة.
- **مزامنة فورية بعد الإرسال:** `GET /api/dashboard/refresh-state` يقدّم `merchant_dashboard_refresh_token` من `CartRecoveryLog` (latest log + latest sent + sent total). `static/merchant_dashboard_lazy.js` يراقب التوكن كل 5 ثوانٍ (no-store) ويعيد جلب `summary` + `normal-carts` + `messages` فقط عند تغيّر التوكن، بحيث رسالة recovery جديدة تظهر فوراً دون hard refresh.
- **`#carts` empty-on-load (V1):** `merchant_dashboard_lazy.js` — لا يعرض «لا توجد سلال» إلا بعد `normalCartsIsConfirmedFullEmpty` (live fetch، `fc.all===0` صريح، غير snapshot/degraded)؛ boot يستدعي `ensureNormalCartsPageReady` ويعيد المحاولة دون الاعتماد على `#completed`.
- **Filter bar persistence (V1):** `merchant_app.js` — اختيار شريط التصفية (sent/attention/…) يُحفظ في `sessionStorage` (`ma_normal_cart_filter_v1`) ولا يُستبدل بـ `#carts?tab=all` عند reapply بعد refresh؛ «الكل» صريح فقط عبر chip أو `goToCartTab('all')`.
- **طبقة قرار D.2:** **`_vip_recovery_decision_layer`** → **`decide_recovery_action(..., is_vip_cart_flag=True)`**؛ لا إرسال قوالب للعميل من المحرك عند هذا العلم.
- **Activation:** **`main._activate_vip_manual_cart_handling`** يضع **`vip_mode`**، **`CartRecoveryLog`** بـ **`status=vip_manual_handling`**، **`try_send_vip_merchant_whatsapp_alert`** (نص: **`build_vip_merchant_alert_body`**؛ هدف: **`store_whatsapp_number`** ثم **`whatsapp_support_url`** القابل للتحليل)، ويضبط **`_session_recovery_sent`** عند النجاح أو عند كان **`vip_mode`** مفعّلاً مسبقاً؛ **`_mark_vip_customer_recovery_closed`** يمنع أي إرسال متابعة للعميل لهذه الجلسة بعد اعتبار السلة VIP في **`handle_cart_abandoned`**.
- **بدون عميل مهما كان تفعيل DB:** إذا **`is_vip_cart`** صحيحة في **`handle_cart_abandoned`** أو **`_run_recovery_dispatch_cart_abandoned_impl`** → لا يُجدول **`multi`** ولا **`_run_recovery_sequence`** كمسار عميل؛ فشل تمييز DB لا يفعّل **fallback** إلى استرداد عميل أوتوماتيكي. في **`_run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned_impl`**: فحص VIP **قبل **`asyncio.sleep`**** لعدم تأخير VIP؛ فحص لاحق دفاعي بعد التأخير يمنع **`send_whatsapp`** للعميل.
- **تنبيه تاجر تلقائي (VIP جديد):** بعد **`cart_state_sync`** / **`cart_abandoned`** عند أول دخول المسار التشغيلي VIP — **`_vip_merchant_auto_alert_if_newly_entering`** → **`_send_vip_merchant_auto_alert`** (يحترم **`merchant_vip_notify_enabled`**؛ يتخطى إن **`vip_notify_enabled=false`**). الإرسال **متزامن** بعد commit مع **poll Twilio** (`poll_twilio_vip_alert_delivery_truth`). **`CartRecoveryLog`** بـ **`reason_tag=vip_merchant_alert`** + حالة **`vip_merchant_alert_accepted|delivered|failed`** (ليس **`sent_real`**). **`resolve_vip_alert_destination`**: **`store_whatsapp_number`** → **`whatsapp_support_url`** → **`CARTFLOW_VIP_ALERT_DESTINATION`**. **`vip_operational_truth_v1`**: استبعاد تنبيهات التاجر من **`sent_count`** / augment / follow-up clarity على **`normal-carts`**. **`GET /dev/vip-merchant-alert-operational-truth`** يعرض **`delivery_truth`** + **`normalized_destination_phone`**. إرسال التاجر يتخطى بوابة قوالب 24 ساعة (**`vip_merchant_alert`** في **`_MERCHANT_ONLY_WA_REASON_TAGS`**).
- **لوحة VIP — قائمة التبويب:** **`GET /api/dashboard/vip-carts`** عبر **`build_vip_dashboard_api_payload`** — batch SELECT VIP carts + bulk reasons/logs، ثم **`vip_dashboard_row_contract`** (بدون N+1؛ لا **`db.session.get`** ولا **`_reason_tag_for_abandoned_cart`** داخل الحلقة). **`GET /dashboard/vip-cart-settings`** وغيرها ما زالت **`_vip_priority_cart_alert_list()`**.
- **لوحة VIP — إرسال يدوي:** **`POST /api/dashboard/vip-cart/{id}/merchant-alert`**؛ سجل **`[VIP MANUAL SEND CLICKED]`**؛ نفس **`try_send_vip_merchant_whatsapp_alert`** مع رسالة UX عربية (**`لا يوجد رقم واتساب للمتجر`** عند انعدام الرقم).
- **اختبار بدون ودجت:** **`POST /dev/create-vip-test-cart`** ينشئ **`AbandonedCart`** ثابت `zid_cart_id=vip-codegen-test-cart-1` (**`cart_value=1200`**, **`vip_mode=true`**, **`status=abandoned`**) + **`CartRecoveryReason`** (**`session_id=test_vip_session`**, **`reason=price`**); يبيّن في قائمة أولوية VIP عند **`interactive`** حقيقية.
- **Logs (جزء):** **`[VIP CHECK]`**, **`[VIP MODE ACTIVATED]`**, **`[VIP CUSTOMER RECOVERY SKIPPED]`**, **`[VIP ACTIVATION FAILED]`**, **`[VIP MANUAL SEND CLICKED]`**, **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT ATTEMPT]`**, **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT SENT]`**, **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT FAILED] reason=…`** (**`vip_merchant_alert.py`**).

---

## 5) End-to-End Flow

**Widget → Backend → Decision → Delay → WhatsApp → Dashboard**

1. User interacts with the layered **V2** runtime (`cartflow_widget_runtime/**`) or legacy **`cartflow_widget.js`** on the storefront; reason persistence follows the active surface (`/api/cartflow/reason` vs `/api/cart-recovery/reason`) → row in **`cart_recovery_reasons`** when applicable.
2. Store platform (or demo) sends **`POST /api/cart-event`** with `event: cart_abandoned`, `store`, `session_id`, optional `cart_id` / `phone`.
3. **`handle_cart_abandoned`**: conversion / duplicate / claim checks → load **`Store`** → **إذا VIP** (`is_vip_cart`): استدعاء **`_vip_recovery_decision_layer`** ثم **`_activate_vip_manual_cart_handling`** ثم **`_mark_vip_customer_recovery_closed`** و**`return`** (لا جدولة إرسال للعميل حتى لو فشل جزء التفعيل).
4. If **multi_message_slots_for_abandon** returns slots → schedule delayed tasks per slot; else **`_run_recovery_dispatch_cart_abandoned`** waits for reason if needed, then schedules **one** delayed **`_run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned`**.
5. After sleep (غير مسار VIP المتوقَّف مسبقاً): **VIP guard** دفاعي؛ ثم رسائل القوالب و**`should_send_whatsapp`** و**`send_whatsapp`** للعميل فقط خارج VIP.
6. **`_persist_cart_recovery_log`** records queued / sent / skipped / VIP rows.
7. **Dashboard** **`GET /dashboard`** — KPIs وأسباب ونشاط من **`AbandonedCart`** / **`CartRecoveryReason`** فقط. **قائمة أولوية VIP** في **`GET /dashboard/vip-cart-settings`** عبر **`_vip_priority_cart_alert_list()`** (الاسم **`_vip_cart_alerts_merchant_list()`** alias للتوافق؛ بدون تكرار في الرئيسية).

---

## 6) Data Models

### `MerchantUser` / auth (`merchant_users`, `merchant_password_reset_tokens`)

`MerchantUser`: `email`, `password_hash`, `merchant_name`, `primary_store_id`. Signup creates a **`Store`** row and sets **`stores.merchant_user_id`** + **`primary_store_id`** (startup DDL via `schema_merchant_auth`); orphan accounts without a store can complete signup with the same email/password. **`POST /signup`** logs **`[SIGNUP 400]`** on validation/register failure. Password reset tokens stored hashed with expiry.

### `Store` (`stores`)

Recovery: `recovery_delay`, `recovery_delay_unit`, `recovery_attempts`, `recovery_delay_minutes`. Optional **`merchant_user_id`** (FK) for SaaS ownership. WhatsApp / UX: `whatsapp_support_url`, `store_whatsapp_number`, `whatsapp_recovery_enabled`, `whatsapp_provider_mode` (merchant dashboard v1 — display/persist; send runtime still uses `config_system` gates), per-reason templates. **VIP (merchant prefs v1):** `vip_enabled`, `vip_notify_enabled`, `vip_note` (display/persist only); **`vip_cart_threshold`** still drives operational lane via `is_vip_cart` / `merchant_vip_threshold_int` (`template_*`, `trigger_templates_json`, `reason_templates_json`), `template_mode` / `tone` / `template_custom_text`, exit intent fields, widget customization (`widget_name`, `widget_primary_color`, `widget_style`). **VIP:** `vip_cart_threshold`.

### `AbandonedCart` (`abandoned_carts`)

`zid_cart_id`, `cart_value`, `status`, URLs, timestamps, **`vip_mode`**, `raw_payload`, optional `store_id`.

### Recovery-related

- **`CartRecoveryReason`** — last widget reason + phones + rejection flags.
- **`CartRecoveryLog`** — recovery audit trail (`status`, `step`, `message`, …); statuses include **`vip_manual_handling`**, **`mock_sent`**, **`skipped_*`**, **`stopped_converted`**, etc.
- **`AbandonmentReasonLog`**, **`ObjectionTrack`**, **`RecoveryEvent`**, **`MessageLog`** — ancillary tracking / webhooks / messaging history as used across routes and webhooks.

---

## 7) Logs & Debugging

| Log / prefix | Where |
|----------------|--------|
| `[CF API]` | `main.handle_cart_abandoned` / cart-event |
| `[VIP OVERRIDE ACTIVATED]`, `[VIP FLOW STOPPED]`, `[VIP CUSTOMER BLOCKED]` | `services/decision_engine.py` (عند `is_vip_cart_flag`) |
| `[VIP CHECK]`, `[VIP MODE ACTIVATED]`, `[VIP CUSTOMER RECOVERY SKIPPED]`, `[VIP ACTIVATION FAILED]`, **`[VIP MANUAL SEND CLICKED]`** | `main.py` |
| `[VIP MERCHANT ALERT ATTEMPT]`, `[VIP MERCHANT ALERT SENT]`, **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT FAILED]`**, **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT TRUTH]`**, **`[VIP MERCHANT AUTO ALERT SENT|SKIPPED|FAILED]`** | `services/vip_merchant_alert.py`, `main._send_vip_merchant_auto_alert` |
| `[DELAY STARTED]`, `[DELAY WAITING]`, `[DELAY FINISHED]`, `[DELAY BLOCKED]` | `main._run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned_impl` |
| `[CARTFLOW DELAY CHECK]`, `[CARTFLOW PRO LOGIC]` | `main.py` |
| `[DELAY CONFIG]` | `services/whatsapp_send.py` |
| `[MULTI MESSAGE *]` | `main.py` |
| `[WA SEND PATH]`, `[WA SEND REASON]`, … | `services/whatsapp_send.emit_recovery_wa_send_trace` |
| `[WA SENT]`, `[WA STATUS]` | `services/whatsapp_send.send_whatsapp` |
| `[BLOCK WA - USER REJECTED HELP]` | `services/whatsapp_send.py` |
| `[SKIP WA - USER REJECTED HELP]`, `[SKIP WA - MISSING REASON_TAG]`, `[SKIP WA - MISSING LAST_ACTIVITY]` | `main.py` |
| `[PHONE RESOLUTION]` | `main._log_phone_resolution` |
| `[WA SENDER MODE]` | `main.resolve_whatsapp_sender` |
| `[PHONE ATTACHED]` | `routes/cart_recovery_reason.py` |
| `[WA REPLY]`, `[WA FROM]` | `main` webhook/whatsapp |
| `[RECOVERY TASK EXIT CLEANLY]`, `[RECOVERY TASK CAUGHT ERROR]`, `[RECOVERY DISPATCH *]` | `main.py` |
| `[ANTI SPAM CHECK]`, `[ATTEMPT CONTROL]`, `[ATTEMPT BLOCKED]`, `[NO VERIFIED PHONE]` | `main.py` |
| `[WHATSAPP TEST]` | `main` dev endpoint |

---

## 8) Known Limitations

- **Two WhatsApp stacks:** Twilio (`send_whatsapp`) for scheduled recovery vs Meta Cloud (`send_whatsapp_message`) for manual cart send — different configuration and behavior.
- **Layer B vs DB:** `config_system` defaults apply when store-specific DB fields are null; merchants must align dashboard **Store** rows and migrations.
- **VIP merchant alert:** depends on **`store_whatsapp_number`** or parsable **`whatsapp_support_url`**, **`vip_notify_enabled`**, and Twilio config; otherwise skip/fail with **`[VIP MERCHANT AUTO ALERT SKIPPED]`** or **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT FAILED]`**. Dashboard **`merchant_vip_alert_state_ar`** is a count badge only — delivery truth is **`CartRecoveryLog`** (`vip_merchant_alert`) + **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT TRUTH]`**.
- **`/webhook/whatsapp`:** minimal handler (prints body); not a full inbound conversation engine.
- **Schema drift:** legacy SQLite DBs need **`schema_widget.ensure_store_widget_schema`** (called from critical paths) so new ORM columns exist.
- **Dual widget bundles:** **default** merchant embed loads **V2** only; **`cartflow_widget.js`** is **explicit rollback** (**`__CARTFLOW_ALLOW_LEGACY_WIDGET`**) or **dev harness** — not the default **`widget_loader`** outcome. **`cartflow_widget.js`** remains large; contributors and **operational tests** still grep **`/api/`** / static markers in **both** trees.

---

## 9) Final Status

| Capability | Status |
|------------|--------|
| Widget → API (reason, config, ready, mock message) | ✅ |
| Detection (Layer B config + store merge) | ✅ |
| Reason capture (`/api/cart-recovery/reason`, `CartRecoveryReason`) | ✅ |
| Persistence (ORM + `schema_widget` + logs) | ✅ |
| Decision engine (D.2 `decide_recovery_action` + template resolution in recovery path) | ✅ |
| WhatsApp send (customer recovery via Twilio gate path) | 🟡 (requires `PRODUCTION_MODE` + Twilio env for real sends; mock otherwise) |
| WhatsApp receive (`/webhook/whatsapp`) | 🟡 (stub / logging) |
| Multi-message (reason templates + scheduled slots) | ✅ |
| Per-reason delay (`get_recovery_delay` + store quiet period in `should_send_whatsapp`) | ✅ |
| VIP (عتبة التاجر فقط، مسار لوحة واحد مقابل عادي، decision-layer override، تنبيه تاجر، لوحة **`vip-cart-settings`** + **`POST …/merchant-alert`**, **`/dev/create-vip-test-cart`**) | ✅ |

**Legend:** ✅ implemented and wired in code · 🟡 partial or environment-dependent · ❌ not implemented

| 2026-07-04 | **Dashboard Read Model Observability v1 (I1+I2+I3+I5 — additive, read-only, no behavior/UI/migration change):** `docs/dashboard_read_model_observability_v1.md`. | 2026-07-04 | **Engineering Constitution v1 established (official engineering standard — docs only, no code):** `docs/engineering_constitution_v1.md`. Defines **how** CartFlow is engineered (not what was built) so the methodology survives changes of developers/maintainers/owners. Ratifies: **§1 Philosophy** (Truth Before Intelligence, Governance Before Optimization, Audit Before Refactor, Measure Before Optimize, Architecture Before Features, Simplicity Before Cleverness, Evidence Before Assumptions, Fail Safe/Fail Loud); **§2 nine-stage Engineering Lifecycle** (Audit→Governance→Contracts→Implementation→Metrics→Enforcement→Institutional Memory→Production Validation→Closure, with rationale for ordering); **§3 Definition of Done** (behavior verified, governance written, contracts defined, metrics available, docs complete, institutional memory updated, production validated, risks classified P0-P3, ownership documented); **§4 permanent Engineering Rules** (one source of truth per question, mint-once/propagate-freely, no hidden writes, archive before delete, `main.py` composes never owns, hot paths never scan history, every growth path measurable, every operational decision observable, every deferred decision documented, generation follows change not clock, fail closed, evidence over assertion); **§5 Architecture Decision Process** (Problem→Evidence→Audit→Governance→Implementation→Measurement→Validation→Closure, no skipping forward, artifacts required); **§6 Quality Gates** (Architecture Review, Regression Classification, Production Validation, Operational Readiness, Metrics, Known-Risk Classification, Institutional Memory, SYSTEM_SUMMARY — AND not OR); **§7 Anti-Patterns** (vibe coding, multiple truth owners, hidden coupling, time-driven rewrites, silent failures, unbounded growth, business logic in composition layers, closing without production validation, optimizing before governing, undocumented deferral, history on hot path, inflated status); **§8 Evolution** (new governance domains added freely via the lifecycle; core clauses change only by formal versioned supersession recorded in decision_registry + this file; precedence: amendment > constitution > subsystem governance > PR conventions). Each principle anchored to real precedents (LT-C1, Purchase Truth, Architecture Consolidation R-01→R-05, Data Growth + Snapshot Generation Governance, Architecture Review Boards V2/V3, Institutional Memory, Production Reality Validation). Includes a constitution-to-practice index. This is the permanent engineering standard future work must implement. No production/behavior/code changes. |
| 2026-07-04 | **Snapshot Generation Governance v1 (durable contracts before optimization — governance only, no code):** `docs/snapshot_generation_governance_v1.md`. Elevates `dashboard_snapshots` generation to a governed truth domain alongside Purchase Truth, Lifecycle Truth (LT-C1), Data Growth, Institutional Memory. Built on `docs/dashboard_snapshot_generation_audit_v1.md`. Defines **10 principles** (P1 change-driven not clock-driven; P2 no identical rewrite; P3 per-type freshness ownership; P4 measurable cost; P5 archive is containment not generation control; P6 cadence never justifies identical rewrite; P7 bounded under unlimited history; P8 hot paths never read snapshot history; P9 explicit per-type freshness; P10 independently evolvable policies) and **12 contracts SG-1…SG-12** (SG-1 generation follows change; SG-2 no identical rewrite via semantic fingerprint; SG-3 history never drives hot reads; SG-4 every write carries a measurable `generation_reason`; SG-5 per-type configurable policy; SG-6 fingerprint over canonical content excluding volatile fields; SG-7 schedule is failsafe not primary trigger; SG-8 generation bounded independent of history size; SG-9 derived snapshots not independently generated (`dashboard_cards`⊂`summary`); SG-10 change detection cheaper than the write; SG-11 explicit freshness contract; SG-12 governance is a reviewable artifact). **Classifies all snapshot types** critical/operational/informational + event/schedule/hybrid trigger (normal_carts=critical/hybrid, summary=critical/hybrid, dashboard_cards=derived-from-summary, refresh_state/widget_panel=event, store_connection=event/informational; reserved monthly_summary/whatsapp_readiness/abandoned_candidates). Defines **meaningful change** (qualifies: lifecycle/purchase/reply/cart mutation/settings/connection/counter-delta/time-window rollover/first-build; does NOT: scheduler tick, TTL elapse w/o change, identical payload, unchanged counters, volatile-only diffs like `generated_at`). Includes future implementation options w/ trade-offs (content hash, per-type policy, event-driven, adaptive scheduling, in-place freshness touch), risks of violating governance, and a reversible behavior-neutral 5-phase migration (shadow observability → SG-2 gate → per-type policy → event triggers → optional CI enforcement). SG-1/2/6/9 flagged as future LT-C1-style gate candidates. No production/scheduler/archive/behavior changes. |
| 2026-07-04 | **Dashboard Snapshot Generation Audit v1 (why `dashboard_snapshots` grows — audit only, no code):** `docs/dashboard_snapshot_generation_audit_v1.md`. Traces the single write path: scheduler-only builder loop (`dashboard_snapshot_loop_v1.py`, default **45s**, floor 15s, single-flight `_tick_lock`) → `run_dashboard_snapshot_builder_tick` → picks up to `STORES_PER_TICK` stores (default **5**, max 50) via stale/oldest priority → `build_store_dashboard_snapshots` writes **all 6 types unconditionally** (summary, dashboard_cards, refresh_state, widget_panel, store_connection + normal_carts). Root cause: `upsert_dashboard_snapshot` (`dashboard_snapshot_v1.py:335`) is **append-only** — reads prev row only for `version+1`, **never compares payloads**; `DashboardSnapshot` has no `(store_slug,snapshot_type)` uniqueness; reads take latest by `generated_at`. **No API-path or event-driven writes** (builder is the only production caller; hot-path guard forbids writes). Findings: growth is **tick-driven, not data-driven**; multiple types rebuilt together (per-type counts ~22,928 each; only `normal_carts` lower ~22,720 because its parity guard can block ~0.9%); "stale" selection = age>300s failsafe, unrelated to data change. Measured prod (2026-07-03): **~42k rows/day** (137,358@01:00Z→153,916@10:22Z), 468 store×type pairs (78 stores×6), avg 293.5 versions/pair over ~3 days (~98/pair/day, ~14.7min interval), **99.66% superseded history**, only **468 rows** ever read. Amplifiers: 6-type co-write + ~78 mostly **test/verify** stores still eligible (only `stuckj-`/`stuckaudit-` excluded). Verdict: architecturally **expected** but content-redundant + volume-unbounded (rate-bounded per tick, not accumulation-bounded). Optimization should target **generation first** (content-hash/change-detection, per-type gating, exclude test stores), **scheduling** second (interval/event-driven; TTLs 30-120s gate reads not builds), **retention** as containment. No code/behavior/scheduler/archive changes. |
| 2026-07-04 | **Production Reality Validation v1 (verify Platform Readiness P0/P1 vs current prod — docs only, no code):** `docs/production_reality_validation_v1.md`. Re-status: **no P0/P1 fully closed** (P0-2 → partially closed); CONTROLLED PILOT READY verdict holds. No production/behavior changes. |
| 2026-07-04 | **Platform Readiness Review v1 (production-SaaS readiness — docs only, no code):** `docs/platform_readiness_review_v1.md`. Ranked P0–P3 risks, production blockers, and 6-/12-month roadmap included. No production/behavior changes. |
| 2026-07-03 | **Lifecycle Truth Enforcement v1 (LT-C1 automated CI gate — enforcement only, no runtime change):** Lifecycle Truth moves from documentation (`docs/lifecycle_truth_contract.md`) to an **executable CI rule**. New pure-stdlib AST gate `scripts/lifecycle_truth_enforcement_v1.py` freezes ownership: the merchant-facing `customer_lifecycle_state` and the `CustomerLifecycleStateV1` truth object may only be **minted** by LT-C1 (`services/customer_lifecycle_states_v1.py`); every other module may **read/propagate** but not invent lifecycle truth ("mint once, propagate freely" — so `.get(...)`/variable/`None` copies in `lifecycle_authority_recovery_v1`, `lifecycle_reconciliation_summary_v1`, `dev_diagnostics`, `main.py` remain legal). Four checks fail the build: **LT-ENF-1** unauthorized mint (canonical state literal / `STATE_*` constant assigned to the field via subscript, attribute, or dict-literal key), **LT-ENF-2** duplicate classifier/attach-helper/`CustomerLifecycleStateV1` class or a function returning it, **LT-ENF-3** external construction of the truth object, **LT-ENF-4** ownership pin (owner must keep defining the classifier/attach/truth object). Distinct classifiers `classify_reply_lifecycle_intent_v1` (reply-intent str) and `classify_merchant_cart_row` (presentation) are explicitly **not** flagged. On violation the gate prints `Lifecycle Truth violation detected. / Unauthorized lifecycle mutation outside LT-C1. / Build rejected.` and exits 1. Wired two ways: GitHub Actions `.github/workflows/lifecycle_truth_gate.yml` (dependency-free `python scripts/lifecycle_truth_enforcement_v1.py`) + pytest `tests/test_lifecycle_truth_enforcement_v1.py::test_current_tree_has_no_violations`. Current tree scan **clean (0 violations)**; tests **25/25 pass**. Doc: `docs/lifecycle_truth_enforcement_v1.md`. No production/lifecycle/scheduler/dashboard/recovery behavior change. |

| 2026-07-03 | **Recovery dispatch timing investigation (investigation only):** `docs/recovery_dispatch_timing_investigation_v1.md` explains why `test_demo_then_demo2_same_session_both_schedule` sees `demo`=`scheduled` but `demo2`=`sent`. Root cause: shared `session_id` + store-agnostic `find_abandoned_cart_for_reason_arm` (session-only match) lets `demo2`'s reason POST materialize+send off `demo`'s abandoned cart before `demo2`'s cart-event, and `get_recovery_delay=0` collapses the async delay so the send completes first; the cart-event then truthfully reports `sent` via `has_sent_truth`. Both dispatch paths are async (`asyncio.create_task`) — not a sync/async branch, and the inline phone is not the cause. Verdict: not a dispatch bug (test over-specified; latent store scoping candidate in reason-arm cart lookup); does not block Architecture Consolidation. No code/behavior changes. |

| 2026-06-06 | **Real demo phone capture + cart visibility truth (runtime break fixed):** True runtime root cause — the synchronous DB-warm hot path (`_ensure_cartflow_api_db_warmed` → `sync_connected_platform_identities`) made a **blocking live HTTPS call to the Zid API per connected store (no aggregate budget, 20s each)** while holding the `db_warm` lock. Tests passed because they run against an isolated DB with no connected-store tokens, so the network was never hit. **Fix:** warm is now offline by default — `sync_connected_platform_identities(allow_network=…)` + `warm_live_platform_sync_enabled()` (opt-in via `CARTFLOW_WARM_LIVE_PLATFORM_SYNC=1`); identity aliases still backfilled offline and refreshed at OAuth time.
